# CHANGES

Substantive behavioral deviations of pypdfbox vs upstream Apache PDFBox.
Per-release notes go here; trivial naming changes (camelCase → snake_case) are not listed.

## Format

```
- pypdfbox/<path>: <one-line description of deviation>
  upstream: PDFBox <version> <java path>
  reason: <why we deviate>
```

## Project-wide deviations vs upstream

- **No `preflight` module.** Apache PDFBox 4.0 removes Preflight; we follow that decision. PDF/A and PDF/UA validation is out of scope — users can plug in any external validator they choose. The pypdfbox repo intentionally has no dependency on, nor scaffolding for, any specific validator (GPL-licensed tools in particular are not used, per PRD §4 forbidden-license list).
- **No commons-logging / log4j.** Python `logging` (stdlib) is used throughout.
- **Method naming.** Java camelCase → Python snake_case across the entire API surface. Semantics unchanged.

## Project status (as of Wave 1389, 2026-05-23)

- **Upstream baseline**: Apache PDFBox 3.0 HEAD (last sync wave 1377).
- **Tests**: 44,400 passing (full pytest with coverage, wave 1390 canonical recipe — 4 deselects, 138 documented skips, 0 deterministic failures).
- **Line coverage**: 99.273% global (124,369 / 125,280 statements; 2,093 excluded; 911 missing — concentrated in `rendering/pdf_renderer.py` 267, `text/bidi.py` 90 [wave 1387 partial], `fontbox/ttf/gsub/lookup_subtable.py` 90, `pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_appearance_generator.py` 89, `util/date_util.py` 50 [wave 1387 partial], `xmpbox/type/oecf_type.py` 45, `pdmodel/font/font_mapper_impl.py` 40).
- **Class parity / method parity**: 1,110 / 1,110 matched classes (100.0%, 0 Java-only after wave 1389 closures of `XrefParser`, `DebugLogAppender`, `GsubWorkerForTamil`) and 8,752 / 8,766 matched methods (99.8%); the residual 14 are debugger Swing inner-class helpers without a direct Tk counterpart.
- **Local TODOs**: 0 in production source (all deferrals tracked in `DEFERRED.md`).
- **Out of scope (permanent)**: `org.apache.pdfbox.preflight.*` (PDFBox 4.0 removed it; PDF/A and PDF/UA validation delegated to whichever external validator the user chooses, per PRD §13).
- **Phase**: Phase 3 closeout. Wave history lives in `HISTORY.md`; open follow-ups live in `DEFERRED.md`.

## Active divergences vs upstream

Divergences that remain live (will affect observable behaviour vs Java PDFBox):

- ~~**ICU bidi reordering not ported.**~~ **Closed wave 1387 (agent A)** — `pypdfbox/text/bidi.py` ships a stdlib-only UAX #9 implementation (`BidiResolver`, `reorder_visually`, `reorder_runs_visually`, `get_paragraph_direction`); `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py::handle_direction` now routes through it (P2/P3 paragraph-direction detection + explicit embedding/override/isolate stack + W1-W7 weak resolution + N0-N2 neutrals + I1-I2 implicit levels + L1-L2 reorder + L4 mirroring). Per-word aggregation in `_emit_group` matches upstream's per-word `handleDirection` contract. No new dependencies.
- ~~**`SimpleDateFormat` locale-sensitive parsing not ported.**~~ **Closed wave 1387 (agent B)** — bundled CLDR-derived month + weekday name tables for the 10 most common locales (en, fr, de, es, it, pt, ja, zh, ko, ru) in `pypdfbox/util/locale_data.py`; new `pypdfbox/util/date_util.py::parse_with_locale` ships a stdlib-only Java SimpleDateFormat tokeniser (yyyy / yy / MMMM / MMM / MM / M / dd / d / EEEE / EEE / HH / H / hh / h / mm / m / ss / s / a / z / quoted-literal) wired into the existing `_SIMPLE_FORMAT_HANDLERS` dispatch table on `DateConverter`. Module-level `to_calendar` falls through to `parse_date` on PDF-regex miss so alpha-start fixtures (`"Friday, January 11, 2115"`, `"Sun, Jul 6, 1980 at 4:23pm"`, `"Friday July 6 17:22:1 GMT+08:00 1979"`, …) parse end-to-end. Diacritic-insensitive (`fevrier` matches `février`) + case-insensitive (`JANUARY` matches `January`) via `unicodedata.normalize` + `casefold`. No new dependencies.
- ~~**Slash-separated `MM/dd/yyyy` date forms not handled.**~~ **Closed wave 1388 (agent A)** — `pypdfbox/xmpbox/date_converter.py::_SIMPLE_FORMAT_HANDLERS` now carries explicit `MM/dd/yyyy`, `MM/dd/yyyy HH:mm`, `MM/dd/yyyy HH:mm:ss` entries matching upstream `Locale.ENGLISH` US-default month-first semantics (the existing `M/d/yy` handler already covered the 4-digit-year shapes via a lenient regex; the new aliases make the dispatch table 1:1 with the commented-out upstream format list at `DateConverter.java` lines 136-142). `D:`-prefix strip routes through the existing `to_calendar` pre-handler. The previously-skipped `test_extract_slash_separated_date_with_optional_time` in `tests/util/upstream/test_date_util.py` now passes.
- **`split_on_space` / `tokenize_on_space` Python regex semantics.** `pypdfbox/util/string_util.py`: `split_on_space("   ")` returns `["", "", "", ""]` (Python's `re.split`); Java's `String.split("\\s")` strips trailing empties and returns `[]`. `tokenize_on_space("   ")` returns `["", " ", " ", " ", ""]`; Java's `Pattern.split` of zero-width lookarounds collapses adjacent matches and returns `[" ", " ", " "]`. Both shapes communicate the same tokens; we record the Python shape.
- **`PDFRenderer` pixel-exact parity not portable.** Upstream JUnit comparisons against stored TIFF/PNG references are *not* ported. Pypdfbox uses Pillow + a skia-backed `_aggdraw_compat` rasteriser; byte-equivalent raster output across the Java AWT and the Python pipeline is unachievable. Affected paths use structural parity (page count, MediaBox, Rotation, Contents shape, Resources keys, save-reload round-trip) anchored to the bundled reference PDFs. `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`.
- **Skia anti-aliasing vs upstream Java2D AA.** The `_aggdraw_compat` skia path may render edge pixels differently from upstream Java2D in low-resolution rasters. Recorded as a known limitation; full pixel parity is not in scope (see preceding bullet).
- **Deeply nested direct containers raise `PDFParseError`, not `RecursionError`.** `pypdfbox/pdfparser/base_parser.py::parse_dir_object`: a malformed PDF nesting direct `[...]` / `<<...>>` past Python's recursion limit (~498-deep arrays at the default limit of 1000) raises the parser's own `PDFParseError` instead of leaking `RecursionError`. Upstream PDFBox is likewise recursive and would throw `StackOverflowError`; it tolerates deeper nesting only because the JVM stack is larger than CPython's recursion limit. Legitimate PDFs nest direct containers only a few levels (logical depth — page/outline/structure trees — uses *indirect* references, which do not recurse), so this guard fires only on hostile input. Found by the wave-1404 malformed-input fuzz harness.
- **Overlong integer literals raise `PDFParseError`.** `pypdfbox/pdfparser/base_parser.py::parse_cos_number`: an integer literal longer than `sys.get_int_max_str_digits()` (4300 by default) raises `PDFParseError` instead of leaking CPython's int-string-conversion `ValueError`. No Java analogue (this is a CPython CPU-DoS guard); pypdfbox-side hardening only.
- ~~**Re-encrypting a loaded-encrypted document double-enciphers stream bodies on save.**~~ — **FIXED wave 1418** (`COSStream.ensure_decrypted()` called from `COSWriter.visit_from_stream`; the 4 double-hop `xfail`s now pass). Original report: Found wave 1409 by the encryption cross-library oracle (`EncryptProbe`/`DecryptProbe`). When a document is loaded encrypted, lazily decrypted (each `COSStream` gets a security handler with `_decrypted=False`), and then re-protected + saved, `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py::visit_from_stream` snapshots the body via `create_raw_input_stream()` — which returns the still-ciphertext bytes (only `create_input_stream()` runs the in-place decrypt pass) — and then enciphers it a second time. The reloaded file's stream bodies are double-encrypted → FlateDecode garbage. Reproduces on flat (non-object-stream) files too, so it is independent of the object-stream decrypt fix in this same wave. **Root cause is in `pypdfbox/pdfwriter`, not encryption** — the writer must decrypt-on-read (or consume the decrypted body) before re-enciphering. The single-hop interop directions (Java-encrypts→pypdfbox-decrypts and pypdfbox-encrypts→Java-decrypts) are unaffected and pass for all four algorithms; only the decrypt-then-re-encrypt double-hop is impacted. Pinned strict-`xfail` in `tests/pdmodel/encryption/oracle/test_encryption_interop_oracle.py::test_double_hop_java_to_py_to_java_preserves_content`.
- ~~**Inline dicts/arrays promoted to indirect objects on full save (object-count inflation).** Found wave 1408 by the writer live-oracle (`SaveRoundTripProbe`). The pypdfbox parser does not call `set_direct(True)` on dictionaries/arrays parsed as *inline* values, whereas upstream `BaseParser.parseCOSDictionary` / `parseCOSDictionaryNameValuePair` do (verified against the pinned 3.0.7 bytecode). Because `COSBase.is_direct()` defaults to `False`, the writer — whose `_write_array` / `_write_dictionary` `is_direct()` branch is byte-for-byte identical to upstream's `writeArray` / `writeDictionary` — emits every inline dict/array as a free-standing indirect object on a full save, inflating the trailer `/Size` (e.g. 347 vs PDFBox's 56 on `unencrypted.pdf`).~~ **Closed wave 1409.** See the Wave 1409 entry below: the parser now flags inline dicts/arrays direct and `COSArray` defaults `direct = True` (mirroring upstream), so the writer keeps them inline; `/Size` now tracks PDFBox within a couple of objects (was ~6×).

## Wave 1446 — TrueType dual-cmap last-wins + inline-image /Interpolate (2 bugs fixed)

- **TrueType `(0,0)`/`(0,3)` cmap promotion was first-wins, not last-wins (FIXED — closes wave-1445 DEFERRED).** `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_true_type_font.py::extract_cmap_table` guarded the `(0,0)`/`(0,3)` Unicode-platform → win-Unicode-slot promotion with `and self._cmap_win_unicode is None`, so for a font carrying BOTH a `(3,1)` and a later `(0,x)` subtable that disagree, pypdfbox kept the `(3,1)` GID where upstream `PDTrueTypeFont.extractCmapTable` assigns the slot unconditionally (last subtable wins). Dropped the guard → last-wins, matching upstream (verified against the 3.0.7 source + live oracle: disputed code `A` → GID 2 not 1). No regression to single-cmap fonts. Pinned in `tests/pdmodel/font/oracle/test_cmap_promotion_oracle.py`.
- **Inline images ignored `/Interpolate` and always upsampled BILINEAR (FIXED).** Found by the new inline-image named-CS oracle (the named-CS resolution itself was already correct — Indexed palette + Separation tint transform from `/Resources /ColorSpace` both resolve). `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_paste_image` hard-coded `Image.Resampling.BILINEAR`, so a small inline raster upscaled into a large device box showed smooth gradients across sample boundaries while PDFBox paints a non-interpolated image with nearest-neighbour (hard pixel edges) — MAD 13.9 on a 2×2 indexed inline image. `_paste_image` gained an `interpolate` parameter (default `True`, backward-compatible) selecting NEAREST when false; `show_inline_image` now reads `inline_image.get_interpolate()` (default false per PDF §8.9.5.3) and threads it through. 1 stale test (a strict-positional `_paste_image` monkeypatch) updated. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_inline_image_named_cs_oracle.py`. Follow-up recorded in DEFERRED: the XObject `Do` paint path still hard-codes BILINEAR and should likewise honour an image XObject's `/Interpolate`.
- Four surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): annotation `/F`-flag render gating (Hidden/NoView suppressed on screen render, Print-only still paints); ExtGState soft-mask `/TR` transfer function (Identity/inverting-Type4/exponential-Type2 — already implemented via a 256-entry LUT); list-box detail (`/TI` top index, sorted `/I`, MultiSelect, `/Opt` export/display, selected-set export-vs-display resolution); remote/embedded GoTo (`GoToR` `/F`+`/D`-as-int/named/array + `/NewWindow` tri-state, `GoToE` `/T` target chain, `Launch` `/Win`).

## Wave 1445 — /W zero-width advance + CCITT byte-align + ActualText + ICC fallback (4 fixes)

- **Type0 `/W` explicit-zero advance was overridden by the embedded hmtx width (FIXED — closes wave-1444 DEFERRED).** `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_draw_glyph` fell back to the embedded program's hmtx advance whenever the declared width was `<= 0`, so a legal `/W` (or `/Widths`) entry of *exactly 0* (e.g. combining marks) was ignored and every following glyph shifted right. Now gates the hmtx fallback on `not self._has_explicit_width(font, code)` (new helper forwarding to the font's `has_explicit_width`) — a present-and-0 width is honoured, a genuinely-absent width still falls back — mirroring upstream `getDisplacement(code).getX()` (PDFBOX-563). Renderer-only root cause. MAXDIFF 115→15. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_zero_width_advance_oracle.py`.
- **`/ActualText` was ignored during text extraction (FIXED).** `PDFTextStripper` captured the marked-content `/ActualText` but never consumed it — `_dispatch` ignored the `BMC`/`BDC`/`EMC` operators entirely (the code's own docstring admitted "not consumed by the default extraction path"). Now the walker dispatches the marked-content operators and a `/Span << /ActualText (...) >>` span's text replaces the glyph-derived text (PDF §14.9.4): emitted once at the span's first show-text run, later runs suppressed, cursor still advanced; UTF-16BE-BOM payloads decode via `COSString.get_string`; `begin`/`end_marked_content_sequence` mirror PDFBox's unconditional-set / peek-clear-pop so nested spans toggle correctly. `/Artifact` text stays included (PDFBox does not exclude artifacts by default). `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py`. Pinned in `tests/text/oracle/test_actual_text_oracle.py`.
- **CCITTFax encode `/EncodedByteAlign` was ignored (FIXED — closes wave-1429 DEFERRED).** The encoder now sets TIFF T4Options bit 2 (`0x4`) for K≥0 (G3 1-D/2-D) so each scanline is byte-aligned; PDFBox's `CCITTFaxFilter.decode` decodes pypdfbox's aligned output back to the original bitmap. K<0 (G4) has no byte-align bit in TIFF's T6Options, so requesting it with K<0 now raises `OSError` instead of silently emitting a non-aligned stream. `pypdfbox/filter/ccitt_fax_decode.py`. Documented residual: PDFBox's own `CCITTFaxDecoderStream` mis-decodes libtiff's byte-aligned G3 output for some run patterns / all G3-2D (upstream decoder limitation — pypdfbox's libtiff decode recovers them exactly).
- **`PDICCBased.to_rgb_image` fell to a per-pixel loop when the embedded profile yields no transform (FIXED).** A LUT-less CMYK ICC profile that LittleCMS rejects dropped to the base class's per-pixel `to_rgb` loop, which re-attempted the already-failed transform once per pixel (a 1000+-line warning storm + O(w·h) slowdown). Now delegates once to the `/Alternate` colour space's bulk `to_rgb_image` (mirrors upstream's `alternateColorSpace.toRGBImage(raster)` short-circuit); output byte-identical. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_icc_based.py`.
- Two surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): alpha-type ExtGState soft mask `/SMask /S /Alpha` (mask derived from the group's *coverage* not luminance — MAD 0, already correct since waves 1384/1386); symbolic simple-TrueType code→GID with no `(3,1)` Unicode cmap ((3,0) raw → (3,0) 0xF000+code → (1,0) Mac fallback chain; a no-cmap symbolic font resolves every code to GID 0 — PDFBox has no "code-as-GID" fallback in `codeToGID`, and pypdfbox matches). A latent `(0,0)`/`(0,3)` cmap-promotion first-wins-vs-last-wins divergence (only when a font has both `(3,1)` and `(0,x)`) is recorded in DEFERRED.

## Wave 1444 — Type1 flex glyphs via create_with_pfb rendered blank (1 bug fixed)

- **Type1 flex / hint-replacement glyphs rendered blank through the in-memory `create_with_pfb` path (FIXED).** Found by the new Type1-flex render oracle. `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/type1_char_string.py::Type1CharString.__init__` built the underlying fontTools `T1CharString` from the program but never attached the parent font's `/Private /Subrs`, so fontTools' `op_callsubr` did `self.subrs[index]` with `subrs is None` → `TypeError`, which `get_path`'s broad `except` swallowed → empty path. Every real `.pfb` reaches flex (OtherSubrs 0/1/2) and hint replacement (OtherSubr 3) via `callsubr`, so any curved flex glyph (`o`/`e`/`s`/…) drawn through the in-memory `create_with_pfb` path rendered blank. Fixed by attaching the font's subrs (a new `_font_subrs_as_charstrings` helper) to the `T1CharString` when not already present — the embedded `/FontFile` reload path (which already attached them) is untouched, and both paths now produce a byte-identical flex outline. `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/type1_char_string.py`. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_type1_flex_render_oracle.py` (+ a curved-flex `.pfb` fixture).
- Five surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): CIDFontType2 `/CIDToGIDMap` STREAM (2-byte big-endian CID→GID, in-range explicit-zero, out-of-range→GID 0, rendered glyphs); annotation appearance `/AP /N` `/BBox`+`/Matrix`→`/Rect` mapping (PDF §12.5.5 transformed-bbox → scale-to-fit, incl. rotation + non-uniform aspect); even-odd vs nonzero FILL (`f*`/`B*`/`b*` honour the even-odd winding — concentric rects leave a hole, self-intersecting star); Indexed colour space with a `/Lookup` STREAM (RGB base exact, CMYK base clamp-identical with the documented CMM tolerance, index clamp to `[0,hival]`); text-field flag + metadata accessors (`/Ff` bit→predicate matrix — multiline/password/comb/doNotScroll/fileSelect/readOnly/required/noExport — + `/MaxLen`/`/TU`/`/TM`/`/Q`).

## Wave 1443 — CropBox render + CalGray + font-factory dispatch + stroke patterns (9 bugs fixed)

- **`PDFRenderer.render_image_with_dpi` rasterised the whole MediaBox instead of cropping/offsetting to the CropBox (FIXED).** Found by the new page-box render oracle (`oracle/probes/PageBoxRenderProbe.java` `render` mode). `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` sized the output image from `page.get_media_box()` and passed the media box as the device-CTM anchor, so a page with a smaller, non-zero-origin `/CropBox` rendered at full media dimensions with no crop-origin offset — upstream `PDFRenderer.renderImage` sizes and anchors to the **crop** box (the rendered image spans the crop window, a non-zero-origin crop shifts the painted content, and `/Rotate` swaps the crop — not media — width/height). On a 400×400 media / 250×200 crop fixture pypdfbox emitted 400×400 (MAD 34.4, MAXDIFF 204) vs PDFBox's 250×200. Fixed by resolving `render_box = page.get_crop_box()` once and threading it through both the pixel-dimension sizing and the `draw_page(image, render_box)` anchor; the existing CTM `translate_origin` (built from `page_size`'s lower-left) now offsets a non-zero-origin crop, and the rotation matrix (built from `page_size`'s width/height) compounds correctly with the crop. Post-fix: cropped page 250×200 MAD 0.0, `/Rotate 90` + 340×250 crop → 250×340 MAD 0.0. Pages without an explicit `/CropBox` are unaffected (`get_crop_box()` returns the media box). Also resolves a latent inconsistency: `render_page_to_graphics`'s anisotropic-resize path already used the crop box for target dims while `render_image` used the media box. Pinned in `tests/pdmodel/oracle/test_page_box_oracle.py`.
- **`PDFontFactory.create_font` dispatched 5 cases wrong (FIXED).** Found by the new font-factory oracle (`FontFactoryProbe`). (1) A `/Type1` or `/MMType1` whose `/FontDescriptor` merely *contains* a `/FontFile3` now dispatches to `PDType1CFont` regardless of the FontFile3 `/Subtype` (was: only when `/Subtype == Type1C`, so a `/FontFile3 /OpenType` or subtype-less FontFile3 went to the wrong class) — mirrors upstream `containsKey(FONT_FILE3)`. (2)+(3) A top-level `/CIDFontType0` or `/CIDFontType2` dict now raises `OSError("Type N descendant font not allowed")` (was: returned a font/None) — matching upstream's `IOException`. (4) An unknown/unrecognised `/Subtype` now falls back to `PDType1Font` with the upstream-shaped warning (was: returned `None`). (5) Added the `fixType0Subtype` descendant-repair step before wrapping a `/Type0`. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_factory.py`; 4 stale tests re-pinned.
- **Stroke tiling/shading patterns + tiling step (2 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new stroke-pattern oracle. (1) A tiling/shading pattern set as the *stroking* colour (`/Pattern` CS + `SCN /P` then a stroked path) painted the stroke band SOLID — the renderer ignored `stroke_pattern`; now builds a stroked-outline alpha mask (`_build_skia_path_stroke_mask`, honouring cap/join/miter/dash) and routes it through the pattern helpers (`_paint_pattern_stroke`). (2) A tiling pattern whose `/XStep`/`/YStep` differ from its `/BBox` tiled wrongly — the cell was *scaled* to the step and top-aligned; now the full `/BBox` cell renders at true device scale, bottom-aligned, clipped to the step-sized tile (matching upstream's `TexturePaint` over the `(XStep,YStep)` anchor rect) with a y-flip lattice-phase correction, so gapped steps show background between tiles and overlapping steps clip correctly. `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (pattern-paint path only, disjoint from the crop-geometry hunks); 1 stale test re-pinned.
- **`PDCalGray.to_rgb` missing the `isWhitePoint()` pass-through (FIXED).** Found by the new CalRGB/CalGray oracle (`CalColorProbe`). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_cal_gray.py` always ran the calibrated CIE pipeline, so a non-unit `/WhitePoint` (e.g. D65) returned wrong RGB (up to 3/255 off; gray 0.25 → 61 vs PDFBox 64). Now mirrors upstream: return `(A,A,A)` verbatim when the white point is not the unit tristimulus, and in the calibrated branch feed the gamma-decoded value to the sRGB conversion as X=Y=Z (PDFBox does not apply the white point there). `PDCalRGB` already matched. The calibrated XYZ→sRGB step stays on pypdfbox's explicit IEC-D65 matrix (vs PDFBox's AWT CMM/D50) — the established documented colour divergence.
- Surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): page-box accessors (`get_media_box`/`get_crop_box`/`get_bleed_box`/`get_trim_box`/`get_art_box`/`get_rotation` + the absent-box→CropBox→MediaBox default chain); embedded-file detail (`/F`/`/UF` unicode, `/AFRelationship`, `/Params` size/dates/MD5-checksum/subtype, decoded content, catalog `/AF` linkage); `/Differences` encoding (`DictionaryEncoding` base+differences override precedence, no-`/BaseEncoding` default to StandardEncoding, code→name→Unicode text) — with one DOCUMENTED cross-module width divergence (a non-trivial `/Differences` flips `is_standard14()` false in both libs, so width falls to `get_width_from_font`; PDFBox returns the LiberationSans *substitute-program* advance for `Euro`=744 while pypdfbox returns the bundled Adobe Core-14 AFM advance=556 — a FontMapper-substitution concern, not an encoding bug).

## Wave 1442 — stroke text-render width + 16-bit RGB images (2 bugs fixed)

- **Stroke text rendering modes (`Tr` 1/2/5/6) painted glyphs as near-solid blocks (FIXED).** Found by the new text-render-mode oracle. `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_build_stroke_pen` applied the `max(0.5, …)` minimum-width floor and the `/SA` snap-to-1.0 against the *glyph-local* pen width — but skia applies the stroke width in glyph-local coordinates *before* the per-glyph CTM (scale ≈ font size), so at 60 pt a 1-user-unit hairline (correctly 0.017 glyph-local) was floored to 0.5 glyph-local ≈ 30 device px, a solid slab (Tr 1 MAD 112 vs PDFBox). Fixed to compute the floor/snap in device pixels and divide back by the CTM scale → Tr 1 MAD 1.6, Tr 2 MAD 1.2. Fill (Tr 0), invisible (Tr 3), and clip (Tr 7) were already correct. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_text_render_mode_oracle.py`.
- **16-bit-per-component DeviceRGB images rendered blank (FIXED).** `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py::decode_pdimage_to_pil` allowed `/BitsPerComponent 16` only for DeviceGray; a 16-bit DeviceRGB image returned `None` and the renderer's raw-raster fallback also rejected `bpc != 8`, so the image painted nothing. Now decodes 16-bit DeviceRGB (big-endian sample unpack → 8-bit down-shift, honouring `/Decode`), matching PDFBox within the down-shift rounding (MAD<6). 16-bit DeviceGray + 16-bit `/SMask` were already correct; 16-bit DeviceCMYK / other spaces remain unsupported (return `None`, documented). 1 stale test re-pinned (its 16-bit-RGB→None premise is now obsolete; switched to 16-bit DeviceCMYK which is still genuinely unsupported).
- Four surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): TrueType `post` table glyph names (format 2.0 Mac-standard + custom Pascal-string indices ≥258 + reverse name→gid); image XObject ENCODE (`JPEGFactory`/`LosslessFactory` — `/Filter`/`/ColorSpace`/dims/BPC/`/SMask` + alpha extraction; a documented JPEG-RGBA codec-vs-codec render band); content-stream operator robustness (BX/EX unknown-operator suppression, unknown-operator-outside recovery, leftover operands, truncated end-of-stream operator); deep DeviceN `/Attributes` (`/Process` + named components, `/Colorants` attribute dict → per-colorant Separation, `isNChannel`) + Separation `/All`.

## Wave 1441 — CJK predefined CMaps + Type0 code→CID + annotation `/OC` hiding (3 bugs fixed)

- **High-traffic CJK predefined CMaps were not bundled (FIXED — major).** `UniGB-UCS2-H/V`, `UniCNS-UCS2-H/V`, `UniKS-UCS2-H/V`, and `GBK-EUC-H/V` were missing from the curated `pypdfbox/fontbox/cmap/resources/` subset, so `CMapManager.get_predefined_cmap` returned `None` for all of them and a Type0 font using `/Encoding /UniGB-UCS2-H` (extremely common for Chinese/Korean PDFs) silently lost its code→CID mapping. Added the 8 byte-identical Adobe CMap resources from the PDFBox 3.0.7 `fontbox` jar (V variants chain to H via `usecmap`; provenance rows + a NOTICE attribution block added — each file already carries Adobe's BSD-3-Clause terms in its `%%Copyright:` header). The `GBK-EUC-H` mixed-width codespace (leading byte `0x00..0x80` → 1-byte code, `0x81..0xFE` → 2-byte) is oracle-verified.
- **`PDType0Font.code_to_cid` echoed the raw code when the CMap mapped it to CID 0 (FIXED).** The implementation consulted the parent CMap but fell through to the descendant (echoing the raw code) whenever a non-zero code mapped to CID 0; upstream `PDType0Font.codeToCID` is just `descendantFont.codeToCID(code)` and returns the CMap's `toCID` verbatim — so e.g. `0xFFFF` under `UniGB-UCS2-H` is CID **0**, not `0xFFFF`. Rewritten to the upstream hierarchy: `pd_type0_font.py` delegates to the descendant; `pd_cid_font_type0.py` = `parent.get_cmap().to_cid(code)`; `pd_cid_font_type2.py` = same + the `!hasCIDMappings && hasUnicodeMappings → toUnicode(code).codePointAt(0)` fallback. Verified by `javap` disassembly of the pinned jar. Bare descendants with no parent/CMap still identity-pass for unit-test wrappers. 2 stale tests corrected.
- **Annotation `/OC` membership ignored at render (FIXED).** `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_render_annotation` honoured the `/F` Hidden/NoView flags but not the annotation's `/OC` optional-content membership — an annotation belonging to an OFF OCG still painted. Now returns early on a hidden `/OC` OCG/OCMD, mirroring upstream `PageDrawer.showAnnotation`'s `isHiddenOCG(getOptionalContent())` (PDF §8.11.4.3); the wave-1430 OC-visibility helper is reused. `PDAnnotation.get_optional_content()` was already correct — the gap was the render gate. OFF-OCG annotation now MAD 0.05 vs PDFBox (was painted).
- Four surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): Type 1 (function-based) shading render via `sh` (incl. non-identity `/Matrix`; one off-path AWT-context divergence in `type1_shading_context.py` documented — dead code w.r.t. the live renderer); form-XObject `/BBox` clip + `/Matrix` (incl. nested compounding, MAD 0.0); document `/Info` ↔ XMP `/Metadata` reads (each from its own source, no accidental cross-sync); CID-keyed CFF (`CIDFontType0C`) FDSelect (format 0/3) + FDArray per-font-dict local-subr/width selection.

## Wave 1440 — Type1 seac accented composites rendered blank (1 bug fixed)

- **Type1 `seac` (accented composite) glyphs rendered completely blank (FIXED).** Found by the new Type1-seac render oracle — and exactly the wave-1438 TrueType-composite bug in the Type1 charstring path (predicted). A Type1 `seac` charstring composes an accented glyph from a base char + an accent char (both StandardEncoding codes), which fontTools' `T1OutlineExtractor.op_seac` emits as `pen.addComponent(name, transform)` relying on the pen's glyph set — but both render-path recording pens were built with `glyphSet=None`, so `BasePen.addComponent`'s `None[name]` raised `TypeError`, the swallowed error dropped the whole composite, and `é`/`à`/`ñ`/`ç` rendered blank (base + accent both gone). Fixed in two pen handlers: `pypdfbox/fontbox/type1/type1_font.py` (the embedded `/FontFile` `cs.draw` path used by `PDType1Font.get_glyph_path`) gained a `_T1GlyphSet` adapter resolving component names to drawables for fontTools' built-in decomposition; `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/type1_char_string.py` (the in-memory `create_with_pfb` path) gained an `addComponent` override resolving components via the reader's `get_type1_char_string` and replaying the transformed outline. Pixel-perfect with PDFBox 3.0.7 (MAD 0.0). The `op_seac` decode itself was correct — the drop was purely the render-path pen, same root-cause class as wave 1438. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_type1_seac_render_oracle.py` (with `tests/fixtures/fontbox/type1/SeacType1.pfb`, a genuine seac composite).
- Five surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): outline (bookmark) detail (`/Count` open/closed sign + `getOpenCount` + `/C` colour + `/F` bold/italic + dest-vs-action); signature field `/Lock` + `/SV` seed value (SubFilter/DigestMethod/Reasons/required-flags) — and a noted *upstream* bug (`PDSeedValue.getReasons()` throws `ClassCastException` because PDFBox writes `/Reasons` as strings but reads them as names; pypdfbox is spec-correct per Table 234); markup threading (`/Popup` open + `/Parent` back-link, `/IRT` reply target resolution, `/RT`, `/State`+`/StateModel`, `/Subj`, `/CreationDate`); non-form annotation flatten (`PDAcroForm.flatten` is form-field-only on both engines — Highlight/FreeText survive with their `/AP`); document catalog secondary metadata (`/OutputIntents` incl. DestOutputProfile ICC, `/MarkInfo /Marked`, `/Lang`, `/Metadata`, `/Collection /View`).

## Wave 1439 — vertical text render + crypt-filter routing + text region clipping + shading/freetext (7 bugs fixed)

- **Text-markup annotations (Highlight / Underline / StrikeOut / Squiggly) confirmed at parity, including the RENDERED shapes (no bug).** Added a new live oracle (`oracle/probes/TextMarkupProbe.java` write+read modes; `tests/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/oracle/test_text_markup_oracle.py`) that builds one of each subtype with a `/QuadPoints` quad + `/C` colour, calls `construct_appearances()`, saves once, and then (1) compares `/QuadPoints` + `/C` accessors against PDFBox reading the SAME pypdfbox bytes — exact canonical-float parity per subtype; (2) compares the generated `/AP /N` operator sequence + `/BBox` against PDFBox's OWN generation; and (3) the high-value addition — rasterises BOTH the PDFBox-authored and pypdfbox-authored PDFs at 72 DPI and compares the 16×16 luminance grid (highlight fill, underline line, strikeout mid-line, squiggly zig-zag) at the standard render gate. Measured MAD 0.26 / MAXDIFF 4 — the per-subtype shapes are pixel-equivalent to PDFBox. `/QuadPoints`, `/C`, and `/BBox` match EXACTLY on all four subtypes. The three operator-spelling divergences are pre-existing and already documented (highlight transparency-group form XObject `gs gs Do` → inline `gs gs rg … f`; underline/strikeout `CS SC` colour-space pair → device shorthand `RG`; squiggly tiling-pattern form XObject `CS SC cm Do` → inline stroked zig-zag `RG w m l … S`) — all render-identical, so no code change in `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/` was needed. The render oracle proves the divergences are spelling-only, not visual.
- **Radial (Type 3) shading context out-of-range remap fixed to match upstream (1 bug fixed).** `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/radial_shading_context.py::get_raster` set `input_value = self._domain[1]` (high) / `self._domain[0]` (low) when an extended pixel fell beyond the parametric range, but the subsequent colour-table index is `key = int(input_value * factor)` and the table is built over the *normalised* `[0,1]` axis. Upstream `RadialShadingContext.getRaster` (PDFBox 3.0.7) sets `inputValue = 1` / `inputValue = 0` there — so with `/Domain ≠ [0 1]` (e.g. `[0.2 0.8]`) pypdfbox indexed the wrong colour-table entry for extended pixels (`0.8*factor` instead of the last entry). Now matches upstream exactly. The `sh`-operator paint path (`pdf_renderer.py::_paint_radial_shading`) already used `0.0`/`1.0` correctly; this fix aligns the AWT-style context path used by shading-pattern / soft-mask fills. The axial `/Extend` / `/Domain` and the `sh`-operator radial nested-circle (cone) / zero-radius-start cases were verified at parity (no change needed) by the new render oracle (`oracle/probes/RenderProbe.java` reused; `tests/rendering/oracle/test_shading_extend_oracle.py`), which also guards that `/Extend [false false]` differs materially from `[true true]` (extend honoured per-flag).
- **Vertical writing-mode text RENDERED left-to-right — WMode ignored at render time (FIXED — major).** Found by the new vertical-text render oracle (`oracle/probes/RenderProbe.java` reused; `tests/rendering/oracle/test_vertical_text_render_oracle.py`): an `Identity-V` Type0 run rendered as a horizontal row indistinguishable from the `Identity-H` control. `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_show_string` unconditionally advanced the text matrix horizontally (`trans = (1,0,0,1,tx,0)` with `tx = width/1000·fontSize·hScale + spacing`) and never consulted `font.is_vertical()` or applied the position vector — so every vertical (WMode-1) glyph laid out rightward instead of stacking downward. Now mirrors upstream `PDFStreamEngine.showText`: for a vertical font `tx = 0` and `ty = getDisplacement().getY()·fontSize + charSpacing + wordSpacing` (horizontal scaling not applied to vertical advance), and `_draw_glyph` prepends the font's position vector (`get_position_vector(code)`, em units) to the per-glyph text-local matrix so the glyph sits centred in the column. `_draw_glyph` gained a keyword-only `vertical` flag and returns the vertical displacement (`/W2` `w1y`, the wave-1428 metric) as the advance in that mode; the horizontal path is byte-for-byte unchanged. Vertical render now matches PDFBox at MAD ~0.1 / MAXDIFF ~5; the vertical-vs-horizontal control diverges MAD ~8 / MAXDIFF ~92 (well outside the parity gate, proving the glyphs really stack). The vertical *metrics* (`PDType0Font.get_displacement` / `get_position_vector`) were already correct (wave 1428) — this was purely the render-time glyph-advance path. 3 stale `_show_string` unit-test stubs that fixed `_draw_glyph`'s arity were updated to accept the new kwarg.

- **Crypt-filter routing: per-slot `/StmF`/`/StrF` ignored on read + per-object AES salt keyed off the wrong flag (2 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new crypt-routing oracle (`CryptRoutingProbe`, mixed `/StmF`≠`/StrF` with one slot `/Identity`). (1) `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/security_handler.py` `_decrypt_string_if_absent` / `decrypt_stream_in_place` called the raw single-algorithm `self._decrypt(...)` instead of the routing-aware `decrypt_string`/`decrypt_stream` overrides — so a `/StrF /Identity` string was AES-decrypted anyway → `ValueError: data is not a multiple of the block length` on load. Now routes through the per-slot overrides (the base handler delegates to `_decrypt`, so V<4 is unchanged). (2) `compute_object_key` added the AESV2 `sAlT` suffix based on the document-wide `self._aes` (derived from `/StmF` alone), so with `/StmF /Identity` + `/StrF /StdCF (AESV2)` the string got an unsalted key → garbage; added an `aes` override threaded from `_dispatch_decrypt`/`_dispatch_encrypt` (AESV2→True, V2/RC4→False). Mixed-routing files now round-trip both directions with `/Identity`-routed objects cleartext on the wire and `/StdCF`-routed objects enciphered. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/security_handler.py` + `standard_security_handler.py`.
- **`PDFTextStripperByArea` region clipping + empty-region separator (2 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new sort/region oracle (`TextSortAreaProbe`). (1) `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper_by_area.py` used fully-inclusive bounds (`min_x <= x <= max_x and min_y <= y <= max_y`), capturing glyphs on the right/bottom edge that PDFBox's `java.awt.geom.Rectangle2D.contains` (half-open) drops — corrected to `min_x <= x < max_x and min_y < y <= max_y` (the y-flip of the device-space half-open box). (2) an extracted region that captured no glyphs returned `""` where PDFBox's per-region `writePage` always emits one `"\n"` separator — now appended unconditionally (a no-`/Contents` page still yields `""` on both; a never-extracted region still returns `""` gracefully vs PDFBox's NPE — pre-existing documented divergence). `setSortByPosition` geometric re-sort + page-range extraction were verified at parity (no change). 2 stale tests corrected.
- **`PDFreeTextAppearanceHandler` skipped the `/Rotate cm` when rotation is 0 (FIXED).** Found by the new free-text/line oracle (`FreeTextLineProbe`). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/annotation/handlers/pd_free_text_appearance_handler.py` emitted the `/Rotate` `cm` only under `if rotation:`, but upstream emits `getRotateInstance(0,0,0)` (the identity matrix) unconditionally — so the lite appearance stream was one `cm` token short of PDFBox's. Now emitted unconditionally; the FreeText callout + Line (caption, leader, `/LE` Diamond/ClosedArrow endings) appearance op-sequences match PDFBox (Line byte-for-byte; FreeText skeleton exact, with the documented one-`Td Tj`-per-segment-vs-per-word text-layout divergence).
- Surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): text-markup annotation accessors + generated `/AP` + RENDERED shapes (Highlight fill / Underline / StrikeOut / Squiggly zig-zag, MAD 0.26 — the operator-spelling divergences are pre-existing + render-identical); `setSortByPosition` + page-range; FreeText/Line accessors (`/DA`/`/Q`/`/CL`/`/LE`/`/IT`/`/L`/`/LL`/`/Cap`/`/CP`); axial `/Extend`/`/Domain` + radial cone/zero-radius `sh`-operator cases.

## Wave 1438 — TrueType composite glyphs rendered blank (1 bug fixed)

- **Composite (compound) TrueType glyphs rendered completely blank (FIXED).** Found by the new composite-glyph render oracle (DejaVuSans embedded as CIDFontType2, showing `éàñ` — accented chars are composite glyphs `e`+`acute` etc.; pypdfbox painted 0 pixels vs PDFBox's full glyphs). The renderer's pen bridge (`pypdfbox/rendering/_pen_bridge.py`) overrode fontTools' `BasePen.addComponent` and routed it to the aggdraw pen's `add_component`, which was a deliberate **no-op** — so every composite glyph's component sub-glyphs were silently dropped at render time (and `font.get_path`/`get_normalized_path` likewise returned 0 commands for composites, affecting the glyph cache + structure extraction). Fixed: the bridge now falls back to `BasePen.addComponent` (the default decomposition — transform each component base glyph and replay it through `move_to`/`line_to`/`curve_to`) when the delegate defines no real `add_component` and a glyph set is present; `_make_path_pen` gained an optional `glyph_set`; `PDCIDFontType2.get_path`/`get_normalized_path` now pass the glyph set so composites assemble. Pixel-parity with PDFBox 3.0.7 (`éàñ`, MAD ~0.47). The `fontbox/ttf` glyf composite-assembly code (`GlyfCompositeDescript`/`GlyfCompositeComp`) was inspected and found correct — the drop was purely in the shared render pen bridge. `pypdfbox/rendering/_pen_bridge.py` + `pdf_renderer.py` + `pypdfbox/fontbox/type1/type1_font.py` + `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_font_type2.py`. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_composite_glyph_render_oracle.py`; 1 stale test corrected.
- Five surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): FDF parse + AcroForm import (hierarchical FQN value-transfer + per-type coercion text/choice→COSString, checkbox→COSName); additional actions `/AA` (annotation E/X/D/U/Fo/Bl/PO/PC/PV/PI, field K/F/V/C, page O/C, catalog WC/WS/DS/WP/DP — trigger set + subtype dispatch); CFF/Type2 charstring glyph rendering; optional-content configuration (`/Order` nesting, `/RBGroups`, `/Locked`, `/Usage` view/print state, `/BaseState`-vs-`/ON`/`/OFF` group-state resolution); document merge (page order + AcroForm field collision de-dup `dummyFieldName<N>` + outline + named-dest).

## Wave 1437 — PDF date conversion + AcroForm calc-order (4 bugs fixed)

- **`DateConverter` crashed / mis-parsed offset dates (3 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new date-conversion oracle (`DateConvertProbe` driving upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.util.DateConverter.toCalendar`/`toString` over a 72-case battery). `pypdfbox/xmpbox/date_converter.py`: (1) a brittle `_PDF_LIKE_RE` fast-path called `datetime(...)` directly, so an out-of-range field (sec 60, Feb 31, hour 24, month 13, day 0) raised an uncaught `ValueError` instead of being rejected cleanly — `to_calendar` now routes the non-ISO path uniformly through the lenient `parse_date` dispatcher, mirroring upstream `toCalendar`→`parseDate` (the dead `_PDF_LIKE_RE`/TZ block was removed); (2) `adjust_time_zone_nicely` shifted the wall clock via `add_minutes(-offset)`, double-applying the zone offset so a `+05'30'` date landed 5.5 h off — it now only attaches the offset (net of upstream's `setTimeZone` + `add(MINUTE,-offset)`); (3) `restrain_t_zoffset` used Python's floored `%` where Java truncates toward zero, so `-99'00'` folded to +09:00 instead of −03:00 — now `dividend - HALF_DAY*int(dividend/HALF_DAY)`. The dispatcher routing also fixed `+05'` (missing minutes), `Z05'00'`, and GMT/UTC/named-TZ forms that previously raised. pypdfbox still surfaces a PDFBox-null parse as `OSError`/`None` (the xmpbox throwing contract) — divergence in *form* only, never in which inputs are accepted. 4 stale tests corrected.
- **`PDAcroForm.get_calc_order` collapsed fully-qualified names (FIXED).** Found by the field-hierarchy oracle (`FieldTreeProbe`). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_acro_form.py` wrapped each `/CO` entry in a fresh field with `parent=None`, so the returned fields' fully-qualified names collapsed to bare partial names (`street` instead of `address.street`). Now matches each `/CO` entry against the already-parented field tree (or the field cache), mirroring upstream `PDAcroForm.getCalcOrder`; a `/CO` entry not reachable from `/Fields` is skipped (also matching PDFBox). 4 stale tests corrected.
- Content-stream generation (`PDPageContentStream`) confirmed at parity (no bug): operator + operand token sequence, string escaping (balanced parens, backslash, non-ASCII hex fallback), number formatting (no float32 noise), and colour-operator selection (`g`/`rg`/`k`) all match PDFBox.

## Wave 1435 — text ligatures + image SMask matte + AES-256 SASLprep (3 bugs fixed)

- **Presentation-form ligatures survived in extracted text (FIXED).** Found by the text glyph-drop oracle. `PDFTextStripper._format_positions_ordered` flushed each per-word run through `handle_direction` but never applied `normalize_word`, so Unicode Alphabetic Presentation Form ligatures (e.g. `ﬁ` U+FB01) survived verbatim where upstream `normalizeWord` decomposes them to `fi`/`fl` via NFKC. Now routes the flush through `normalize_word` (which already wraps `handle_direction`), matching upstream's `normalizeWord`→`handleDirection` chain. This was the real content divergence behind the wave-1434 "poems-beads trailing glyphs dropped" deferral — no glyphs were ever dropped (the residual full-document divergence is the separate, still-xfailed `/B` bead reading-order feature). `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py`. Pinned in `tests/text/oracle/test_text_glyph_drop_oracle.py`.
- **Image `/SMask` `/Matte` was ignored during compositing (FIXED).** Found by the SMask-matte oracle. When an image's `/SMask` carries a `/Matte` array (the background colour the image colour was pre-blended against, PDF §11.6.5.3), the base colour must be un-pre-multiplied (`c = matte + (c' − matte)/alpha`). pypdfbox modelled `/Matte` (accessors existed) but never applied it — `PDImageXObject.apply_mask` discarded its `matte` arg and the renderer's SMask path did a plain `putalpha` — so pre-blended colours rendered darkened/fringed where alpha < 1 and the page backdrop differed from the matte. Added `_unpremultiply_matte` in the image SMask path (mirrors upstream `PDImageXObject.applyMask`: skip alpha 0, clamp to [0,255]); MAD 7.4 → pass. SMask `/Decode` inversion and non-8-bpc SMask were already correct. `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`.
- **AES-256 (V5/R6) passwords were not SASLprep-canonicalised (FIXED).** Found by the AES-256/R6 deep-parity oracle (`Aes256R6Probe`). The standard handler UTF-8-encoded the raw R6 password string with no `SaslPrep` step (despite comments claiming otherwise), so a password containing a compatibility character (e.g. the `ﬀ` ligature U+FB00 → `ff`) hashed to different bytes than PDFBox — leaving the file **mutually unopenable** between the two libraries. `get_password_bytes` now applies `SaslPrep.sasl_prep_query` (read) and the encryption-dict prep applies `sasl_prep_stored` (write) for revision 6, mirroring upstream `StandardSecurityHandler`. The eager `str`→UTF-8 encoding in `PDFParser`'s load path and `PDDocument.decrypt` was changed to pass the raw `str` to `StandardDecryptionMaterial` so its revision-aware charset+SASLprep logic runs (also fixes r2–r4 `str` passwords to use Latin-1 per spec). `/Perms` validation, the R6 2.B hardened hash, and `/UE`/`/OE` key recovery were already correct. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/standard_security_handler.py` + read paths in `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py` + `pypdfbox/pdmodel/pd_document.py`.
- Three surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): TrueType cmap subtable selection + code→GID (format-0/4/6/12, platform/encoding priority, symbolic 0xF0xx fallback); viewer preferences + page layout/mode/lang/version (every getter, enum mapping, and absent-key default); multimedia/3D/rendition annotations & actions (fully implemented — the trimmed app jar returns `Unknown`/`null` for several, pypdfbox ports the full source and matches on subtype string + factory dispatch).

## Wave 1434 — embedded font encoding + transparency groups + RC4 revisions (5 bugs fixed)

- **Embedded simple fonts with no `/Encoding` rendered blank (FIXED — major).** Found by the new built-in-encoding oracle (`BuiltinEncodingProbe`, covering an embedded Type1 `/FontFile` and an embedded TrueType `/FontFile2`, each with no `/Encoding`). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_simple_font.py::get_encoding_typed` surfaced the program's built-in encoding only for *non-embedded* Standard-14 fonts (the wave-1431 fix), returning `None` for embedded fonts — so `PDType1Font._code_to_glyph_name` resolved every code to `None` and dropped every glyph (text rendered blank). Now mirrors upstream `PDSimpleFont.readEncoding`: when `/Encoding` is absent it unconditionally falls back to `read_encoding_from_font()` (embedded or not); a *present-but-malformed* `/Encoding` (non-name/non-dict) still resolves to `None`, exactly as upstream leaves it null. Oracle-verified that bare Type1/Type1C/TrueType-no-`/Encoding` resolve `StandardEncoding` in PDFBox; embedded Type1 went from blank to MAD 0.00, all 256 codes' glyph name + width now match. The symbolic-TrueType cmap path is untouched. 20 stale tests that pinned the old `None`/`.notdef` contract were re-pinned to the oracle-verified PDFBox values. Pinned in `tests/pdmodel/font/oracle/test_builtin_encoding_oracle.py`.
- **Transparency-group constant alpha + luminosity-SMask backdrop (2 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new transparency-group oracle (`test_transparency_group_oracle.py`). (1) A group's `/ca` constant alpha was applied to each interior element instead of to the group composite as a whole (PDF §11.6.4.3): an isolated group at `/ca 0.5` scored MAD 14.3 vs PDFBox. `_render_transparency_group` now resets interior GS alpha to 1.0 during the group render and applies the saved `/ca` to the group composite (plus non-isolated backdrop removal, §11.4.8) → MAD 0.33. (2) A luminosity `/SMask` opened uncovered regions per the `/BC` backdrop *luminance* instead of masking them to alpha 0; the oracle proved PDFBox modulates luminosity by the mask group's *coverage* (so `/BC` only tints where the group actually paints). `_render_soft_mask_alpha` now seeds `/BC` at alpha 0 and computes `luminance × coverage` → MAD 64.9 → 0.00. `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`; 3 stale soft-mask tests corrected.
- **RC4 standard-handler revision selection + 40-bit owner-password recovery (2 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new RC4 interop oracle (`Rc4InteropProbe`, R2/R3 × encrypt-decrypt × user/owner). (1) `prepare_document` hardcoded `revision=2` for every 40-bit (`/V 1`) document; upstream `computeRevisionNumber(1)` returns **R3 when any revision-3 permission bit is set** (the default `AccessPermission` sets all four), R2 only when none are. Now derives the revision via `compute_revision_number_from_version(1)`. (2) `get_user_password` (Algorithm 7 inverse) ran the 50-round MD5 loop over the full 16-byte digest instead of the first `key_len_bytes` — identical for 128-bit keys but wrong for a 5-byte (40-bit) key, so a valid owner password was rejected on V1/R3/40-bit documents (a path only reachable after fix #1). Now truncates to the key length, matching upstream `computeRC4key`. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/encryption/standard_security_handler.py`; 5 stale revision tests corrected. RC4 R2/R3 now round-trip both directions (user + owner + owner-only) with matching `/V`/`/R`/`/Length`/`/P`.
- Three surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug): widget/link annotation appearance (`/AS` state resolution, `/AP /N` sub-dict keying, `/MK` BG/BC/caption, `/D` down appearance + `/N` fallback, link `/H`/border); linearization (neither pypdfbox nor PDFBox 3.0.7 *writes* linearized output — both drop `/Linearized` on save; pypdfbox *reads* a real `qpdf --linearize`d file to identical page count + `/Linearized` dict facts + content); named-destination resolution (legacy `/Dests` dict + modern `/Names /Dests` multi-level name tree + link/`OpenAction` named `/D` all resolve to the same page index + fit + coords).

## Wave 1433 — embedded Type1 glyph rendering (1 bug fixed)

- **Embedded Type1 glyphs from an in-memory PFB program rendered blank (FIXED).** Found by the new Type1 glyph-render oracle (`RenderProbe` over an embedded `/FontFile` Type1 font: pypdfbox painted nothing, MAD ~10.6 vs PDFBox). `Type1Font.get_path` / `get_width` called `.draw()` directly on each `/CharStrings` value — which works only when the value is a decompiled fontTools `T1CharString` (the embedded-`/FontFile` reload path), but for an in-memory `create_with_pfb` program the values are raw charstring *bytes* with no `.draw`, so the `AttributeError` was swallowed and every outline came back `[]` / every advance `0.0` (glyph dropped). Both methods now detect a non-drawable value and route it through pypdfbox's own Type1 charstring interpreter (`get_type1_char_string` → `Type1CharString`: full `hsbw`/`rmoveto`/`rlineto`/`rrcurveto`/`closepath`/`seac`/flex/`OtherSubrs`). Missing-glyph semantics (`[]`/`0.0`, no `.notdef` fallback) preserved. `pypdfbox/fontbox/type1/type1_font.py`. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_type1_glyph_render_oracle.py` + `tests/fontbox/type1/test_type1_font_get_path_bytes_wave1433.py`.
- Five surfaces confirmed at parity (no bug, new differential coverage): image-XObject `/Decode` inversion + `/ImageMask` stencil paint (explicit/`colour-key`/`SMask` already covered wave 1429); text-field appearance generation (DA font+size, quadding L/C/R, comb `/MaxLen`, multiline wrap, auto-size — benign divergences documented: auto-size clamps to 12pt vs upstream ~17.3pt cap-height, colour op `0 g` vs `cs/sc`, multiline one `Tj`/line vs one `Tj`/word); page labels (decimal/Roman/letter styles + prefix + `/St` start, incl. 4→iv / 27→AA overflow); interactive actions (URI/GoTo/GoToR/Launch/Named/JavaScript string+stream/SubmitForm/ResetForm + `/Next` chain); tagged-PDF structure-element detail (role-map resolution, attribute objects, class names, mixed `/K` MCID/element/OBJR kids).

## Wave 1432 — image render flip + inline stencils + broken-file recovery (5 bugs fixed)

- **Every rendered image was vertically flipped vs PDFBox (FIXED — major).** Found by the new inline-image render oracle (a hand-authored, vertically-*asymmetric* image rendered upside-down vs Java; reproduced through a full pypdfbox writer round-trip of an asymmetric XObject too). `PDFRenderer._paste_image` applied an unconditional extra `transpose(FLIP_TOP_BOTTOM)`, but the page device CTM already bakes in the user-space y-flip — so every painted image (inline *and* XObject) was double-flipped. The whole existing render-oracle corpus missed it because those fixtures use vertically-symmetric images. Removed the extra flip (`pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`); 2 stale unit tests that had codified the upside-down orientation were corrected.
- **Inline `/IM true` image masks were not painted in the fill colour (FIXED).** `show_inline_image` lacked the `is_stencil()` branch the XObject `Do` path has, so a 1-bit inline stencil decoded as opaque DeviceGray (black where it should take the non-stroking fill colour, opaque where it should be transparent). Routed inline stencils through the existing `_paint_stencil_mask`. Pinned (with the flip fix) in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_inline_image_oracle.py`.
- **Broken-file recovery: missing/wrong xref was not brute-force recovered (3 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new recovery oracle (`RecoveryProbe` over a 2-page PDF corrupted three ways — garbled `startxref`, deleted xref table+trailer, wrong subsection offset; PDFBox brute-force-recovers all three, pypdfbox did not). (1) A missing/unlocatable xref+trailer raised `missing 'startxref' directive` instead of recovering; `PDFParser.parse` now falls back to `_rebuild_document_from_brute_force()` (scans `n g obj` headers, rebuilds the trailer, registers table entries) in lenient mode. (2) A wrong xref subsection offset stranded the object; added `_check_xref_offsets_lenient()` / `_object_header_matches()` mirroring upstream `COSParser.checkXrefOffsets` (verify each offset points at its `n g obj` header, brute-force-correct mismatches). (3) The rebuild path now eagerly dereferences recovered objects (`_resolve_recovered_objects()`, mirroring `BruteForceParser.searchForTrailerItems`) so a body-level defect surfaces as a load-time failure exactly as upstream. Located-but-malformed xref *streams* still raise (unchanged strict contract — verified: the malformed-xref-stream rejection guards stay green). `pypdfbox/pdfparser/pdf_parser.py` + `cos_parser.py`.

## Wave 1431 — mesh shadings + Standard-14 AFM metrics (3 bugs fixed)

- **Mesh shadings (Type 4/5 free-form/lattice Gouraud) rendered completely blank; Type 6/7 (Coons/tensor patch) banded (FIXED — major).** Found by the new mesh-shading oracle (`RenderProbe` over `sh`-filled mesh PDFs: PDFBox painted a full corner gradient, pypdfbox MAD ~140 — nothing drawn). `PDShadingType4.collect_triangles` / `PDShadingType5.collect_triangles` were stubs returning `[]`, so the renderer had no triangles to paint. Implemented the bit-packed mesh decoders (free-form flag-driven for Type 4, lattice row-major for Type 5, reusing the existing `_PatchBitReader`/`_interpolate`) and a renderer painter `_paint_triangle_mesh_shading` using skia `drawVertices` for true Gouraud interpolation. Type 6/7 patch meshes were additionally banded because the rasteriser flat-averaged each triangle's corner colours and `_calc_patch_level` only subdivided on geometry — added a colour-variation subdivision floor + per-vertex Gouraud triangle fill (`_fill_skia_gouraud_triangle`). Type 4/5 now MAD ~1.1; Type 6/7 MAD ~6.4 (a documented residual ~4-luminance uniform offset — pypdfbox interpolates the patch colour field over a Gouraud cell grid, PDFBox per pixel; the gradient is smooth, not banded). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/shading/pd_shading_type{4,5}.py` + `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py`. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_mesh_shading_oracle.py` (all 4 types + blank-page guards). The previously-deferred Type 4/5 triangulator is now removed from deferred scope.
- **Non-embedded Standard-14 fonts returned a flat 250-unit width for every glyph (FIXED — major).** Found by the new direct-AFM oracle (`Std14MetricsProbe`, building each of the 14 core fonts via `new PDType1Font(FontName.X)` — no PDF, no `/Widths`, AFM-only). `PDSimpleFont.get_encoding_typed()` returned `None` for a font with no `/Encoding` entry (the established lazy contract), but `PDType1Font.get_standard14_width(code)` reads the per-glyph AFM advance through that typed encoding — so a bare `PDType1Font.HELVETICA` resolved every code to `.notdef` and `getWidth`/`getStringWidth` collapsed to the 250 substitute width. Fixed `get_encoding_typed`'s no-`/Encoding` branch to resolve the built-in encoding via `read_encoding_from_font()` for non-embedded Standard-14 fonts (mirrors upstream `PDSimpleFont.readEncoding`'s `else` branch). The established `None` contract is preserved for every other no-`/Encoding` font (bare/embedded/non-Standard-14). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_simple_font.py`.
- **Standard-14 Latin default encoding was StandardEncoding, not WinAnsiEncoding (FIXED).** `PDType1Font.read_encoding_from_font` returned `StandardEncoding.INSTANCE` for the twelve Latin core fonts, but the live PDFBox 3.0.7 oracle proves `new PDType1Font(FontName.HELVETICA).getEncoding()` is `WinAnsiEncoding` — Acrobat treats the unembedded core fonts as WinAnsi regardless of the bundled AFM's declared `EncodingScheme AdobeStandardEncoding`. The two encodings disagree on dozens of codes (39→`quotesingle` 191 not `quoteright` 222; 96→`grave` 333 not `quoteleft` 222; 128→`Euro` 556; 160→`nbspace`→`space` 278; the entire 0xC0-0xFF accented range), so the wrong default produced the wrong AFM advance for every disagreeing code. Symbol/ZapfDingbats correctly keep their FontSpecific built-in encodings. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type1_font.py`. After both fixes, per-code `getWidth`, font BBox, and ascent/descent/capHeight/xHeight/italicAngle match PDFBox 3.0.7 exactly for all 14 fonts; the only `getStringWidth` divergence is the pre-existing documented encode-leniency boundary (PDFBox raises `IllegalArgumentException` on an unencodable glyph, pypdfbox substitutes). Pinned in `tests/pdmodel/font/oracle/test_std14_metrics_oracle.py`.

## Wave 1430 — CFF widths + DCT CMYK pipeline + optional-content render visibility (5 bugs)

- **Optional-content (OCG/OCMD) visibility was never evaluated during rendering (FIXED — major).** Found by the new render-time OC oracle (`RenderProbe` at the default render state). `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` never dispatched the `BMC`/`BDC`/`EMC` marked-content operators at all, and the OC-visibility predicates (`is_content_rendered`, `is_hidden_ocmd`) were hardcoded stubs — so content inside an OCG whose default config marks it OFF rendered **identically to an ON layer**, and a form/image XObject carrying an OFF `/OC` entry still painted. Wired up the marked-content operators + an OC-visibility gate (`_is_content_rendered` resolving an OCG's default-config ON/OFF state and an OCMD's `/P` policy + `/VE` expression), and guard all painting (fills, strokes, glyphs, inline images, shadings, image/form XObjects) on it until the matching `EMC` — mirroring upstream `PageDrawer`'s `nestHiddenOCG` / `isContentRendered`. `page_drawer.py` delegate stubs now route to the renderer helpers. Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_optional_content_render_oracle.py` (OCG ON/OFF marked content, XObject `/OC`, OCMD AnyOn) with a flip-ON guard proving visibility is actually evaluated.
- **CFF/Type1C width-from-font + built-in encoding (3 bugs FIXED).** Found by the new CFF subset oracle (`CffSubsetProbe`, the `/FontFile3` sibling of wave-1429's TrueType `SubsetProbe`). (1) `CFFFont.get_encoding_map()` did not exist, so `PDType1CFont.read_encoding_from_font` always fell back to `StandardEncoding` instead of the embedded CFF program's built-in encoding (codes like 2→`fi`, 16→`caron` resolved wrong) — added it (surfaces fontTools `top.Encoding` as `{code: name}`). (2) `PDType1CFont.get_width_from_font` resolved codes only via the dict `/Encoding` (returns `None` when absent → width 0.0); now mirrors upstream `getEncoding()`'s built-in fallback plus a `.notdef`/`defaultWidthX` fallback for glyphs absent from a subset. (3) `PDCIDFontType0._cff_program_width` gated on `has_glyph` (which `CFFCIDFont` reports `False` for CID 0/.notdef) and rejected zero advances, returning 0 for CID 0; CID-keyed programs now take the width straight from the CID per upstream `PDCIDFontType0.getWidthFromFont`. `getWidthFromFont` for every addressed code now matches PDFBox 3.0.7 across real CIDFontType0C + Type1C subsets. Benign: PDFBox's float font-matrix transform emits sub-unit width noise (e.g. `778.0001`) — compared at whole-1/1000-em resolution.
- **`/DCTDecode` CMYK images bypassed the PDF colour pipeline (FIXED).** Found by the new DCT oracle (`JpegImgProbe`). The DCT branch in `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/image/pd_image_x_object.py` did `Image.open(...).convert("RGB")` for *every* JPEG, sending CMYK through Pillow's opaque, version-dependent LittleCMS path and bypassing the PDF `/ColorSpace` entirely. Now `_dct_jpeg_to_rgb` keeps the fast path for gray/RGB but routes a CMYK codestream under a `/DeviceCMYK` space through `PDDeviceCMYK.to_rgb_image` (the deterministic transform every other DeviceCMYK raster uses), keeping the JPEG path consistent + Pillow-version-stable. Polarity was already correct (Pillow un-inverts Adobe APP14 on read, so the `/Decode` array must not be re-applied — re-applying double-inverts). Gray/RGB are pixel-tight; the residual CMYK luminance gap is the pre-existing documented subtractive-CMYK-vs-ICC `PDDeviceCMYK` divergence. Pinned in `tests/pdmodel/graphics/image/oracle/test_dct_decode_oracle.py` (gray, YCbCr RGB, CMYK+APP14).

## Wave 1429 — rendering oracle round-out (pattern fills + transparency)

- **Tiling-pattern `/Matrix` ignored when painting a pattern fill (FIXED).** Found by the new pattern-fill live oracle (`RenderProbe` over a PaintType-1 tiling pattern carrying a `1.5x` scale + `(12, 8)` translate `/Matrix`: pypdfbox MAD ~64 / MAXDIFF ~205 vs PDFBox — the lattice tiled from the canvas origin at the page CTM scale, in completely the wrong place and size). `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_paint_tiling_pattern` derived the cell pixel size from `_full_ctm()` (page CTM only) and pasted tiles from canvas `(0, 0)`, never consulting `pattern.get_matrix()`. Upstream anchors the tile lattice in the pattern's own space — `Matrix.concatenate(getInitialMatrix(), pattern.getMatrix())` — so a translating/scaling `/Matrix` shifts the lattice phase and changes the device-space cell size. Fixed to compute `pattern_device_ctm = matmul(pattern_matrix, self._device_ctm)` (deliberately *not* folding in `self._gs.ctm`, which the pattern matrix is defined to ignore), derive per-axis device scale from its column norms for the tile pixel size, and offset the paste loop by the device-space position of the pattern-space cell origin (lattice phase). Matrix case drops to MAD ~4.9 / MAXDIFF ~26 (within the wave-1408 AA gate); the identity-matrix colored/uncolored/shading fills are unchanged (paths that previously matched still match). Pinned in `tests/rendering/oracle/test_pattern_fill_oracle.py` (PaintType-1, PaintType-2-uncolored-via-`scn`, PaintType-1+`/Matrix`, axial shading pattern) with a solid-fill guard that proves the MAD gate catches a pattern-to-flat-fill regression. Reuses the existing `oracle/probes/RenderProbe.java`.

## Wave 1428 — flatten / vertical writing / clipping oracle parity (3 surfaces, 3 bugs fixed)

- **`PDAcroForm.flatten` left widgets without a drawable appearance behind (FIXED).** Found by the new live oracle (`FlattenProbe`). `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/form/pd_acro_form.py::_flatten_widget` skipped removing a widget from its host page's `/Annots` whenever the widget had no `/AP /N` stream (e.g. an unset text field) — leaving dangling interactive annotations after flatten. Upstream `PDAcroForm.flatten` removes every mapped widget regardless of appearance (`AcroFormsBasicFields.pdf` left 2 widgets, `MultilineFields.pdf` left 3; Java leaves 0). Fixed to resolve the host page, render the appearance only when present, then unconditionally remove the widget. Three stale unit tests that asserted the buggy "no appearance ⇒ keep" behaviour were corrected. Benign retained divergence: on flatten-*all* pypdfbox drops the now-empty catalog `/AcroForm` dict outright where upstream keeps it with an empty `/Fields` — both leave zero referenceable fields + zero widgets, so the "form is gone" contract is identical. Pinned in `tests/pdmodel/interactive/form/oracle/test_flatten_oracle.py`.

- **`PDType0Font.get_displacement` vertical branch used the wrong metric (FIXED).** Found by the new live oracle (`VerticalFontProbe`, `PDType0Font.getDisplacement` / `PDCIDFont.getVerticalDisplacementVectorY`). For a vertical (`/WMode 1`) font, `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_type0_font.py::get_displacement` returned `(0, descendant.get_height(cid)/1000)` — the glyph's *vertical extent* (`yMax−yMin`), which also falls back to `0.0` for CIDs not covered by `/W2`. Upstream `PDType0Font.getDisplacement` returns `(0, descendantFont.getVerticalDisplacementVectorY(code)/1000)`: the `/W2` `w1y` advance metric, falling back to the displacement-vector-y component of `/DW2` (spec default `−1000`). Every vertical displacement was wrong — covered CIDs returned the glyph extent instead of `w1y`, and un-covered CIDs returned `0.0` instead of `−1.0`. Fixed to call `descendant.get_vertical_displacement_vector_y(code)` (passing the raw code, which the descendant resolves to a CID itself, mirroring upstream). `is_vertical` (WMode-1 detection), `get_position_vector` (`/W2` `(v_x,v_y)` scaled `−1/1000`, `/DW2[0]=880` default), and `get_vertical_displacement_vector_y` already matched the oracle and are unchanged.
  - Note: `PDCIDFontType2.get_height` (glyph extent `yMax−yMin`) still diverges from upstream's `PDCIDFontType2.getHeight` (`(ascender−descender)/unitsPerEm`); it is a separate glyph-extent accessor unrelated to vertical advance and out of this wave's `/W2` surface — left as-is, documented here for the next pass.

- **Line dash / cap / join (`d` / `J` / `j` / `M`) ignored when set inline in a content stream, and never applied at stroke time (FIXED).** Found by the new clipping/line-style live oracle (`RenderProbe` over a dashed-stroke PDF: pypdfbox MAD 7.64 / MAXDIFF 146 vs PDFBox's dashed reference — a *solid* line). Two gaps: (1) `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` had no dispatch entries for the `J` (line cap), `j` (line join), `M` (miter limit) or `d` (dash) content-stream operators — they were silently dropped, so only the `gs` ExtGState path (`/LC` / `/LJ` / `/ML` / `/D`) ever set them; (2) the skia stroke paint (`_aggdraw_compat.Draw._make_stroke_paint`) only set colour + width, so even an ExtGState-set cap/join/dash never reached `skia.Paint`. Added the four operator handlers (`_op_line_cap` / `_op_line_join` / `_op_miter_limit` / `_op_set_dash`) + dispatch rows; extended the `Pen` shim with `line_cap` / `line_join` / `miter_limit` / `dash` and a `_make_stroke_paint_from_pen` that maps them onto `Paint.setStrokeCap` / `setStrokeJoin` / `setStrokeMiter` and `skia.DashPathEffect`; `_draw_via_aggdraw` and `_build_stroke_pen` (stroked glyphs, Tr 1/2/5/6) now plumb the GS stroke style through. Dashed-stroke parity drops to MAD 1.62 / MAXDIFF 18 (AA on the dash-segment edges). Clip (`W` / `W*`), nested-clip restore, and text-clip (`Tr 7`) already matched PDFBox to MAD ≤ 0.50.

## Wave 1427 — license-gate hardening + crypt-filter / marked-content oracle parity

(3 of 6 planned surfaces this wave — AcroForm flatten, vertical writing, and clipping-path agents hit the account session limit and were reverted clean; re-run in wave 1428.)

- **License gate hardened (defense-in-depth, closes the wave-1420 follow-up)**: `scripts/check_native_licenses.py` scans installed native artifacts (`.so`/`.pyd`/`.dylib` + `dist-info/licenses/` SPDX grant lines) for copyleft markers (GPL/AGPL/LGPL/MPL/EPL/CDDL/SSPL/BUSL) and Rust cargo-registry crate paths — catching the jbig2-style "MIT metadata hiding a GPL `.so`" the metadata-only `pip-licenses` gate is blind to. Word-boundary matching + a justified 2-entry allow-list (numpy's gcc-runtime libs under the GCC Runtime Exception / LGPL dynamic-link) avoid the known false positives. Wired as **gate 3** in the local `.git/hooks/pre-push` (after ruff + pip-licenses) and documented in `CLAUDE.md`. Current env: 441 artifacts scanned, clean. Tested (`tests/test_native_license_scan.py`) incl. a synthetic-violation flag.
- **crypt filters + metadata encryption (parity confirmed, no bug)**: `CryptFilterProbe` — `/StmF`/`/StrF`/`/CF` + `CFM` names, `isEncryptMetaData`, and `/EncryptMetadata false` cross-library round-trips (pypdfbox↔Java; metadata stream stays cleartext + recovers) all match across AES-128/256; `/Identity` crypt-filter routing respected. (PDFBox 3.0.7 lacks `setEncryptMetadata`, so the Java→py md-off direction is pinned at R6 — documented.)
- **marked content (parity confirmed, no bug)**: `MarkedContentProbe` — `BMC`/`BDC`/`EMC`/`MP`/`DP` operator sequence + inline-dict vs `/Properties`-name property operands + the `PDFMarkedContentExtractor` tag/MCID/nesting tree match Java exactly across 6 tagged fixtures + a synthetic all-operator content stream.

## Wave 1426 — JBIG2 port: document/page assembly + filter wiring (JBIG2 decoding RESTORED)

Final wave of the `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` port — the top-level assembly and `/JBIG2Decode` filter wiring. **JBIG2 image decoding is restored, permissively (no GPL, no native code).**

- **`JBIG2Document` + `JBIG2Page`** (`pypdfbox/jbig2/`): parse the JBIG2 stream (both the embedded organisation — PDF, bare segments + external globals — and the standalone file organisation), resolve referred-to + global segments, and compose the page bitmap from its region segments (default pixel value + per-region blit with the combination operator + striping). Ported `segments/Table` (custom Huffman table, type 53) and wired the segment-type dispatch in `segment_header.py` to all ported types (no `NotImplementedError` stubs remain). `Jbig2PageProbe` end-to-end oracle: `JBIG2Document(...).get_page(1).get_bitmap()` is **bit-exact vs the bundled Java decoder** on 003.jb2 (2550×3305), 005.jb2 (2544×3330), 006.jb2 (2496×3337), and **21.jb2 + 21.glob** (2560×3296 — embedded organisation, external globals, striped page).
- **`/JBIG2Decode` filter re-wired** (`pypdfbox/filter/jbig2_decode.py`): `decode` reads `/JBIG2Globals` from `/DecodeParms`, decodes via `JBIG2Document`, and inverts to the DeviceGray 1-bpp convention (sample 0 = black) matching upstream `JBIG2Filter`/`Bitmaps.buildRaster`. **Bit-exact vs Java at both levels**: the raw `FilterDecodeProbe JBIG2Decode` output (1,054,295 bytes identical) and the image level (`PDImageXObject.get_image()` vs PDFBox `getImage()` — 16×16 fingerprint identical, delta 0) on 003/005/006. Re-added the JBIG2 filter decode tests (removed in wave 1420) + an image-level oracle. `jbig2_filter.py` docstring updated (supported, not "unsupported"). README + docs/install updated.
- `JBIG2ImageReader` (the upstream `javax.imageio.ImageReader` SPI entry point) is **deferred** — entirely coupled to the Java ImageIO framework and not needed for the PDF filter path (which calls `JBIG2Document` directly). A large-symbol-dictionary edge case (805 symbols, `20123110001.jb2`) hits a residual divergence and is deferred (see `DEFERRED.md`); the common decoder paths (generic/text/symbol/halftone/refinement, embedded+globals, striped) are all bit-exact.

The 6-wave port (1421–1426) restores `/JBIG2Decode` with first-party Apache-2.0 Python, replacing the forbidden GPL `jbig2-parser` (wave 1420). Every layer is differential-tested against the bundled Java JBIG2 plugin; ~470 tests in `tests/jbig2/`.

## Wave 1425 — JBIG2 port: text region (last decoder) + symbol-dict aggregate path

Fifth wave of the `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` port — `TextRegion` (§6.4), the final and most complex decoder. Places symbol instances from a symbol dictionary onto a region bitmap: strip/instance positioning (STRIPT/FIRSTS/CURS, IADT/IAFS/IADS/IAIT/IAID + Huffman equivalents), transposed/reference-corner placement, combination operator, per-instance refinement. `TextRegionProbe` reflectively drives the bundled Java `TextRegion` against the symbols of a referred symbol-dictionary segment from the real fixtures — **bit-exact** on full-page text regions: 003.jb2 (2550×3305) and 005.jb2 (2544×3330). Also completed (un-stubbed) the `SymbolDictionary` aggregate-decoding path (§6.5.8.2) now that `TextRegion` exists.

+18 tests (430 total in `tests/jbig2/`). All JBIG2 segment decoders are now ported and oracle-verified. Final wave: `JBIG2Document`/`JBIG2Page` + full `Bitmaps` page assembly + `JBIG2ImageReader`, wire the segment-type dispatch, re-wire `pypdfbox/filter/jbig2_decode.py` to the Python decoder, and the end-to-end image-level oracle.

## Wave 1424 — JBIG2 port: pattern dictionary + halftone region + symbol dictionary

Fourth wave of the `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` port — the dictionary/halftone decoders.

- **`PatternDictionary`** (§6.7) + **`HalftoneRegion`** (§6.6): pattern dict decodes a collective bitmap (`GenericRegion`) sliced into HDPW×HDPH patterns; halftone decodes Gray-coded grayscale planes and renders by placing patterns. `PatternDictionaryProbe`/`HalftoneRegionProbe` reflection oracles: pattern **6/6 bit-exact**, halftone **5/5 bit-exact** on placements where the bundled 3.0.7 jar and the (newer) ported upstream agree. Documented version divergence: the refactored upstream fixes 3.0.7's HGX/HGY double-add in `renderPattern` and adds the PDFBOX-6156 `Bitmaps.blitByPixel` slow path; oracle scoped to agreeing placements, divergent ones unit-tested. Also ported `image/bitmaps.py` primitives (`extract`/`combine_bytes`/`blit`) and the `Dictionary` interface.
- **`SymbolDictionary`** (§6.5): height-class/delta-width symbol decoding — arithmetic direct + single-instance-refinement paths and the full Huffman path (collective bitmaps via `Bitmaps.extract`) fully ported; SBSYMCODELEN, IAID, export-flag run-length, imported-symbol + user-table resolution. `SymbolDictProbe` decodes the real upstream `.jb2` fixtures' standalone symbol-dict segments via reflection — **bit-exact on 003.jb2 (99 symbols) + 005.jb2 (305 symbols)**. The aggregate-decoding path (>1 aggregation instance, §6.5.8.2) raises `NotImplementedError` pending `TextRegion` (wave 1425). Fixtures `003.jb2`/`005.jb2` copied from upstream test resources.

+61 tests (412 total in `tests/jbig2/`). Next: `TextRegion` (the last decoder), then `JBIG2Document`/`JBIG2Page` + full `Bitmaps` page assembly + `JBIG2ImageReader`, then re-wire `pypdfbox/filter/jbig2_decode.py` + the image-level oracle.

## Wave 1423 — JBIG2 port: generic + generic-refinement region decoders

Third wave of the `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` port — the two base region decoders.

- **`GenericRegion`** (`pypdfbox/jbig2/segments/generic_region.py`, JBIG2 §6.2): arithmetic (templates 0–3, GB context + AT pixels + TPGDON typical-prediction) and MMR decode paths → `Bitmap`. `GenericRegionProbe` drives the bundled Java `GenericRegion` via reflection on a crafted generic-region segment; **16 oracle cases bit-exact** (templates 0–3 nominal/AT-override/TPGDON, byte-aligned + non-aligned widths, MMR mode).
- **`GenericRefinementRegion`** (`pypdfbox/jbig2/segments/generic_refinement_region.py` + `decoder/generic_refinement_region_decoding_procedure.py`, §6.3): refines a reference bitmap with templates 0/1 + TPGRON. **`RefinementProbe` oracle: 6 cases bit-exact** for the paths the bundled 3.0.7 jar and the newer upstream share. NOTE: we ported the *refactored* upstream (separate decoding-procedure class), which fixes/changes 3 things vs the older inlined 3.0.7: (1) TPGRON no longer NPEs on the first SLTP (3.0.7 bug); (2) template-1 uses dedicated explicit/TPGR line routines; (3) AT override activates unless *both* coords == -1 (and AT2 always samples the reference bitmap). The oracle is scoped to the agreeing paths; the rest is unit-tested and will be covered by the image-level oracle when the pipeline is wired. `_get_gr_reference`'s no-referred-segments branch depends on the not-yet-ported `image.bitmaps` (later wave).

+76 tests (351 total in `tests/jbig2/`). Next: document/page dispatch, pattern-dictionary + halftone, symbol-dictionary + text-region, then image assembly + reader + filter wiring.

## Wave 1422 — JBIG2 port: Huffman + MMR coders + segment-header structure

Second wave of the `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` port. Both entropy coders are **bit-exact vs the bundled Java decoder**:

- **Huffman** (`pypdfbox/jbig2/decoder/huffman/`): `HuffmanTable` + `Code`, `StandardTables` (all 15 standard tables B.1–B.15 verbatim), `FixedSizeTable`, `EncodedTable`, the prefix-tree nodes (`Node`/`InternalNode`/`ValueNode`/`OutOfBandNode`). `HuffmanProbe` oracle: 66 cases (all 15 tables × bit patterns + multi-value sequential decodes) **match Java exactly**, including the OOB sentinel and negative/32-bit range lines.
- **MMR** (`pypdfbox/jbig2/decoder/mmr/`): `MMRConstants` (white/black/mode run-length code tables verbatim) + `MMRDecompressor` (2-D MMR/T.6 Group-4 decoder → `Bitmap`). `MmrProbe` oracle: 8 cases over real CCITT-G4 strips (pass/horizontal/vertical modes, makeup runs, byte-aligned + non-aligned widths) — decoded bitmap **bit-exact vs Java** (dims + every packed byte).
- **segment structure** (`pypdfbox/jbig2/`): `SegmentHeader` (full §7.2 header parse), `SegmentData`/`Region` interfaces, `segments/RegionSegmentInformation` (§7.4.1), `segments/PageInformation` (§7.4.8), `segments/EndOfStripe`, `segments/Profiles`. `SegHeaderProbe` oracle confirms header fields (number/type/page-assoc/referred-to/lengths) parse identically to Java. The segment-type → data-class dispatch raises `NotImplementedError` for the region/dictionary types still to be ported (waves ahead).

+147 tests (275 total in `tests/jbig2/`). Next: document/page + segment dispatch, then region decoders, symbol/text, image assembly + reader, then re-wire the filter.

## Wave 1421 — begin porting `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` to Python (Apache-2.0): foundation layer

Restoring `/JBIG2Decode` with a permissive decoder by porting the Apache-2.0, pure-Java `apache/pdfbox-jbig2` (the decoder upstream PDFBox itself uses) to a new `pypdfbox/jbig2/` package (mirrors `org.apache.pdfbox.jbig2`). This replaces the GPL `jbig2-parser` removed in wave 1420 — first-party Python, no native code, no new dependency. The JBIG2 plugin is bundled in the pinned `pdfbox-app-3.0.7.jar`, so each ported piece is differential-tested against the real Java decoder. Wave 1421 = the self-contained foundation:
