Files touched: `pypdfbox/cos/cos_array.py` (+13 lines), `pypdfbox/pdfparser/cos_parser.py` (+27 lines), `pypdfbox/fontbox/cff/char_string_command.py` (+15 lines), `tests/cos/test_cos_array_wave1388.py` (new), `tests/pdfparser/test_cos_parser_wave1388.py` (new), `CHANGES.md` + `DEFERRED.md` (this entry).
- **Agent C — verify + reframe the wave-1387 "residual zero-contour `space` glyph" note as upstream parity (not a divergence).** The wave-1387 Agent E narrative described "the lone residual `space` at code 0x20 is zero-contour by design — correct in original Adobe Symbol too" but the framing could read as a documented gap. Wave 1388 Agent C verified the parity claim against upstream PDFBox 3.0.x source and locked it under explicit assertions. **Upstream evidence:** (1) `pdfbox/src/main/resources/org/apache/pdfbox/resources/afm/Symbol.afm:43` declares `C 32 ; WX 250 ; N space ; B 0 0 0 0 ;` — zero bounding box implies zero contours, with advance width 250; (2) `pdfbox/src/main/resources/org/apache/pdfbox/resources/afm/ZapfDingbats.afm:43` declares `C 32 ; WX 278 ; N space ; B 0 0 0 0 ;` — same zero-contour shape with advance width 278; (3) upstream `org.apache.fontbox.ttf.TrueTypeFont.getPath` (TrueTypeFont.java:768-783) returns `new GeneralPath()` when the GID has no outline and explicitly comments *"some glyphs have no outlines (e.g. space, table, newline)"*; (4) upstream `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.font.Standard14Fonts.getGlyphPath` (Standard14Fonts.java:271-306) returns `new GeneralPath()` as its terminal fallback when the substitute font carries no outline for the requested glyph name. Our `Standard14Fonts.get_glyph_path('Symbol', 'space')` returns `[]` — byte-for-byte parity with `new GeneralPath()`. Advance widths are preserved on the `Standard14FontWrapper.get_width('space')` path (250.0 for Symbol, 278.0 for ZapfDingbats), so text-width measurement is correct: a space rendered through Adobe Symbol takes up the upstream-correct 250-unit advance despite emitting no pixels — exactly what Java PDFBox does. **Reframing:** Symbol + ZapfDingbats coverage is at parity with Adobe's original Standard 14 cores — including the upstream-standard zero-contour space glyph (renders as advance-width only, matching the original Adobe font and matching upstream Java PDFBox). No "Active divergences vs upstream" entry needed (this is parity, not divergence) and the wave-1387 coverage stats stand: 188/189 Symbol drawable + 187/188 ZapfDingbats drawable, with the single `space` exclusion intentional and upstream-faithful. Anchored by `tests/pdmodel/font/test_symbol_dingbats_space_parity_wave1388.py` (new, 9 hand-written tests: encoding pin for code 0x20 on both fonts, AFM advance-width pin against `Symbol.afm`/`ZapfDingbats.afm` row 43 byte-values, `Standard14Fonts.get_glyph_path` empty-list pin on both with upstream-`getGlyphPath` rationale in the assert message, `Standard14FontWrapper.get_width`/`.get_path` parity pin showing the advance survives while the path stays empty, and an end-to-end aggregate test tying encoding + AFM + runtime through a single consistent story). All 9 new tests pass; all 5,475 `tests/pdmodel/font/` tests pass (25 pre-existing skips unchanged). No new Python dependencies. No camelCase aliases. No `# noqa` suppressions added. Files touched: `tests/pdmodel/font/test_symbol_dingbats_space_parity_wave1388.py` (new), `CHANGES.md` (this entry).

## Wave 1387 — close documented-divergence retentions

- **Agent B — locale-sensitive `SimpleDateFormat` parsing (closes the long-standing "`SimpleDateFormat` locale-sensitive parsing not ported" divergence).** Pre-1387 `pypdfbox/xmpbox/date_converter.py::parse_simple_date` was regex-driven for digit-start patterns only; the seven `ALPHA_START_FORMATS` shapes (Java's `"EEEE, MMM dd, yy"`, `"EEEE, MMM dd, yy 'at' hh:mma"`, `"EEEE MMM dd HH:mm:ss z yy"`, etc.) silently fell through. PDFs carrying Acrobat Distiller / GNU Ghostscript creator dates (`"Wed, January 11, 2215"`, `"Sun, Jul 6, 1980 at 4:23pm"`, `"Friday July 6 17:22:1 GMT+08:00 1979"`) reached `DateConverter.to_calendar` and either raised `OSError` ("Invalid date format") or — for shapes carrying a leading digit — got mis-parsed by the looser big-endian branch. Wave 1387 closes the gap with a stdlib-only port: (1) **`pypdfbox/util/locale_data.py`** (new, ~155 LoC) bundles CLDR-derived month + weekday name tables for the 10 most common locales — **en, fr, de, es, it, pt, ja, zh, ko, ru** — covering full + abbreviated month names (12 × 2 per locale) and full + abbreviated weekday names (7 × 2 per locale) for ~520 strings total; exposes `get_month_names_full` / `get_month_names_abbrev` / `get_weekday_names_full` / `get_weekday_names_abbrev` / `SUPPORTED_LOCALES`. (2) **`pypdfbox/util/date_util.py`** (new, ~340 LoC) ships `parse_with_locale(input_str, pattern, locale="en") -> datetime | None` — a self-contained Java SimpleDateFormat tokeniser handling `yyyy` / `yy` (with the standard `[today-79, today+20]` sliding window) / `MMMM` / `MMM` / `MM` / `M` / `dd` / `d` / `EEEE` / `EEE` / `HH` / `H` / `hh` / `h` / `mm` / `m` / `ss` / `s` / `a` (AM/PM marker) / `z` (TZ designator placeholder) / `'…'` (single-quoted literal). Pattern letters that repeat (Java's `EEEEEEEEEE` / `MMMMMMMMMMMM` from upstream `TestDateUtil`) collapse to the shortest matching token per Java semantics. Field-width parsing is lenient (`dd` accepts 1..2 digits at parse time — strict-2-digit applies only on format, matching Java's `SimpleDateFormat` parse-side lenience). Greedy longest-match: `MMM` walks both abbreviated *and* full month names and picks the longer hit, so `EEEE, MMM dd, yy` matches both `"Monday, Jan 11, 1915"` (3-char month) and `"Friday, January 11, 2115"` (7-char month). Diacritic-insensitive (`fevrier` matches `février`, `Marz` matches `März`) + case-insensitive (`JANUARY` matches `January`, `MONDAY` matches `Monday`) via `unicodedata.normalize("NFKD", …)` + `casefold()`. (3) **Dispatch wiring** in `pypdfbox/xmpbox/date_converter.py` — new `_make_handler_locale(fmt)` adapter wraps `parse_with_locale` into the existing `(text) -> (cal | None, consumed_chars)` `_SIMPLE_FORMAT_HANDLERS` contract; new `_make_handler_locale_split_at_tz(fmt)` variant splits patterns containing `" z"` (TZ-designator placeholder) so the pre-`z` field group parses via `parse_with_locale`, the embedded TZ blob routes through the existing `parse_t_zoffset` for offset extraction (without `adjust_time_zone_nicely` — wall-clock fields stay as written), and the post-`z` year tail parses via a second `parse_with_locale` call. All seven `ALPHA_START_FORMATS` shapes are now wired into `_SIMPLE_FORMAT_HANDLERS`. (4) **`to_calendar` fallback** — when the PDF-regex `_PDF_LIKE_RE.match(date)` returns `None` for alpha-led input (the `date[0].isdigit()` guard), the module-level `to_calendar` now delegates to a new `_try_parse_date_fallback` which invokes `DateConverter.parse_date` and enforces upstream's full-consumption rule (`where.index == len(text)` after dispatch — exactly upstream's `toCalendar` line 731 check, which is how it rejects e.g. `"20070430193647+713'00' illegal tz hr"`). (5) **ISO fractional-minute edge case** — `_from_iso8601` strips `HH:MM.fff` (millis spliced between minute and TZ) via a new `_ISO_FRACTIONAL_MINUTE_RE` per upstream PDFBOX-1219 behaviour. Wave 1387 also unskips six previously-skipped tests at `tests/util/upstream/test_date_util.py` (`test_check_parse_iso_with_milliseconds_after_minute`, `test_check_parse_pdfbox_465_ambiguous_digit_shapes`, `test_check_parse_weekday_month_name_shapes`, `test_check_parse_dd_mmm_yyyy_shapes`, `test_check_parse_named_tz_with_textual_date`, `test_check_parse_ambiguous_big_endian_date`); only one skip remains in the file (slash-separated `MM/dd/yyyy` form, explicitly out of scope per the original divergence note). Anchored by `tests/util/test_locale_date_format_wave1387.py` (new, 453 hand-written tests: per-locale × per-month full + abbreviated round-trip parametrise sweep (10 × 12 × 2 = 240 tests), per-locale × per-weekday full + abbreviated round-trip parametrise sweep (10 × 7 × 2 = 140 tests), table-integrity sweep (40 tests across 10 locales × 4 categories), case-insensitive sweep (10 tests across MIXED / lower / Title / mIxEd case), diacritic-folding sweep (8 tests across French / German months + Spanish weekdays), unknown-locale-falls-back-to-English (1 test), empty + unparseable + missing-year + trailing-residue rejection (4 tests), upstream-fixture-shape sweep (6 tests), AM/PM marker handling (3 tests including the 12:00am → hour=0 normalisation). No new Python dependencies. No camelCase aliases. No `# noqa` suppressions added. All 750 `tests/util/` tests pass (1 unrelated skip retained for the slash-separated form); all 3,307 `tests/util/` + `tests/xmpbox/` tests pass; broader 25,466-test sweep across `tests/util/` + `tests/xmpbox/` + `tests/pdmodel/` green. Files touched: `pypdfbox/util/locale_data.py` (new), `pypdfbox/util/date_util.py` (new), `pypdfbox/xmpbox/date_converter.py` (locale-handler dispatch + `to_calendar` fallback + `_from_iso8601` fractional-minute strip), `tests/util/test_locale_date_format_wave1387.py` (new), `tests/util/upstream/test_date_util.py` (six skip-stub bodies replaced with live upstream-fixture assertions). `uv run ruff check` clean.

- **Agent A — port the Unicode Bidirectional Algorithm (UAX #9) and wire it into `PDFTextStripper::handle_direction` (closes the long-standing "ICU bidi reordering not ported" divergence).** Pre-1387 `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py::handle_direction` was a single-line `word[::-1] if any R/AL else word` heuristic — pure-LTR runs short-circuited correctly but mixed-LTR+RTL paragraphs (an Arabic word inside an English sentence, a Hebrew quote with a Latin number) emitted a whole-string reversal that scrambled the LTR sub-runs against their source order; the documented divergence accepted this loss because Python's stdlib has no ICU equivalent. Wave 1387 closes the gap with a stdlib-only port: **`pypdfbox/text/bidi.py`** (new module, ~430 LoC) ships `BidiResolver.resolve(text, paragraph_direction=None) -> list[int]` implementing the full UAX #9 spec — P1-P3 paragraph-direction detection (first-strong-character scan, isolate-aware), X1-X10 explicit embedding / override / isolate stack (LRE / RLE / LRO / RLO / PDF / LRI / RLI / FSI / PDI with `MAX_DEPTH = 125` per §3.3.2, overflow-isolate + overflow-embedding counters, FSI sub-string scan via `_fsi_substring_direction`), W1-W7 weak-type resolution (NSM inherits, EN-after-AL → AN, AL → R, single ES/CS between EN/EN → EN, ET-adjacent-to-EN → EN, separators → ON, EN-preceded-by-L → L), N0-N2 neutral resolution (NI sequence takes surrounding-strong direction; AN/EN count as R for surroundings; N2 fallback to embedding direction), and I1-I2 implicit-level resolution (even-level R → +1, AN/EN → +2; odd-level L/EN/AN → +1). The reorder layer ships `reorder_visually(text, levels)`, `reorder_runs_visually(runs, levels)` (mirrors Java's `Bidi.reorderVisually(byte[] levels, int levelStart, Object[] objects, int objectStart, int count)` contract for parallel-array reordering of `TextPosition` lists), `get_paragraph_direction(text)`, and a module-private `_reorder_indices` helper implementing L2 (reverse all level runs ≥ highest level, iterate down to the lowest odd level). L1 (paragraph + segment separator + trailing-whitespace reset) lands inside `BidiResolver.resolve`. L4 (Unicode mirroring) lives in `PDFTextStripper.handle_direction` via a 35-entry `_BIDI_MIRROR_MAP` covering ASCII brackets (`()`, `[]`, `{}`, `<>`), French / German guillemets (`«»`, `‹›`), mathematical delimiters (`⌈⌉`, `⌊⌋`, `⟨⟩`, `⟪⟫`), and CJK paired punctuation (`「」`, `『』`, `【】`, `〔〕`, `〖〗`, `〘〙`, `〚〛`, `《》`, `〈〉`); the bracket map covers every codepoint typically encountered in PDF text extraction (the Unicode `BidiMirroring.txt` resource carries the canonical full table, but the heavy tail past these 35 is rarely encountered in practice — additions are a one-line append). The integration in `pdf_text_stripper.py` rewires `_emit_group` to buffer text per word (accumulating adjacent `TextPosition` fragments between word breaks) and run `handle_direction` once per word — matches upstream Apache PDFBox's per-word `handleDirection` contract in `LegacyPDFStreamEngine.normalize` (PDFTextStripper.java:2100). The buffer flushes at every word separator, line separator, and paragraph break. The fast path (`!has_strong_rtl && !has_explicit_format`) returns input unchanged so pure-LTR extraction has zero per-word overhead. Mirroring fires only on RTL-level codepoints whose `unicodedata.mirrored` flag is True. Test coverage: `tests/text/test_bidi_wave1387.py` (new, 34 hand-written tests covering paragraph-direction detection across 6 cases, pure-LTR / pure-RTL / mixed-paragraph resolution + reorder, W2 / W7 number-after-AL and number-after-L semantics, "12 abc 34" embedded-LTR-run preservation inside an RTL paragraph, L1 trailing-whitespace reset, `reorder_visually` / `reorder_runs_visually` contract pinning including the length-mismatch error and the 2-level nested-run reorder, `handle_direction` integration — ASCII unchanged, empty-input, pure-Arabic reverses, mixed-paragraph keeps LTR run in source order, Arabic numerals come through, `(abc)` bracket-mirror under L4, BidiSample fixture round-trip idempotency). `tests/text/upstream/test_bidi.py` ported tests `test_sorted` / `test_not_sorted` updated with refreshed skip reasons documenting that BiDi is closed but the lite stripper's line-break heuristic (Y-coordinate threshold) does not split the bundled fixture's tightly-packed positions across the expected one-line-per-case layout — a separate, documented residual. `tests/text/test_pdf_text_stripper_bidi_paragraph_wave1370.py` (test for the old whole-reverse behaviour) updated to pin the new UAX #9 semantics on the same inputs; the explicit "ICU paragraph reordering is out of scope" placeholder test (previously `pytest.skip`-only) is replaced with a live assertion against the new behaviour. No new Python dependencies. No camelCase aliases. No `# noqa` suppressions added. Files touched: `pypdfbox/text/bidi.py` (new), `pypdfbox/text/pdf_text_stripper.py` (`handle_direction` rewrite + `_emit_group` per-word buffer + `_BIDI_MIRROR_MAP` module table + import wiring), `tests/text/test_bidi_wave1387.py` (new, 34 tests), `tests/text/upstream/test_bidi.py` (skip-reason refresh), `tests/text/test_pdf_text_stripper_bidi_paragraph_wave1370.py` (whole-reverse test updated to spec-compliant expectation; ICU-divergence placeholder converted to live assertion). All 842 `tests/text/` tests pass (4 unrelated skips); all 23,496 `tests/contentstream/` + `tests/pdmodel/` tests pass; all 3,244 `tests/rendering/` + `tests/multipdf/` + `tests/examples/` tests pass. `uv run ruff check` clean.

- **Agent E — lift Adobe Symbol substitute coverage from 84% to 100% via PUA-name synthesis fallback (closes the wave-1380 audit residual).** The wave-1380 audit of `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/standard14_fonts.py::_LIBERATION_TTF_NAMES` recorded a 158/189 = 83.6% Adobe Symbol coverage gap with the bundled DejaVu Sans substitute. The 31-glyph shortfall is the set of Adobe-specific Private-Use-Area codepoints (U+F6D9..U+F8FE) for bracket-extension pieces (`parenlefttp`, `bracketleftex`, `bracerightmid`, …), the serif/sans variants of register / copyright / trademark, and the horizontal/vertical extension bars for stretchable arrows and integrals. Wave 1387 investigated every permissively-licensed math-symbol font on the OFL/MIT/BSD/Apache allow-list — **STIX Two Math** (2.13, OFL), **DejaVu Math TeX Gyre** (2.37, Bitstream Vera + public domain), **Noto Sans Math**, **Asana Math**, **Pagella Math** — and confirmed *none* target the Adobe-Symbol PUA codepoints by codepoint *or* by Adobe's PostScript glyph name (verified per-codepoint via fontTools cmap probes; STIX Two Math hit 3/32, DejaVu Math TeX Gyre 3/32, both via the two non-PUA `angleleft`/`angleright` codepoints + `space`). The Adobe PUA scheme is unique to Adobe Symbol; modern OpenType math fonts use OpenType `.s1`/`.s12` size variants exposed through GSUB rather than PUA codepoints — bundling another font would not help. Instead wave 1387 adds a **synthesis fallback table** `_SYMBOL_PUA_FALLBACKS: dict[str, int]` (32 entries; the 31 PUA names + a no-op identity for completeness) that maps each Adobe-Symbol PUA name to its nearest **base glyph** in the already-bundled DejaVu Sans: bracket-extension pieces collapse to the base bracket character (`parenlefttp` → `(` U+0028, `bracketrightbt` → `]` U+005D, `braceex` → `|` U+007C), angle brackets route to the modern BMP MATHEMATICAL ANGLE BRACKET pair (`angleleft` → U+27E8, `angleright` → U+27E9 — DejaVu Sans does not carry the deprecated U+2329 / U+232A but does carry the math pair), stretchable-line extension parts flatten to ASCII bars (`arrowvertex` / `integralex` → `|`, `arrowhorizex` → `—` U+2014, `radicalex` → `‾` U+203E), and the serif / sans register / copyright / trademark variants collapse to the single Unicode mark (`registerserif` / `registersans` → `®`, `copyrightserif` / `copyrightsans` → `©`, `trademarkserif` / `trademarksans` → `™`). The fallback is wired into `Standard14Fonts.get_glyph_path` as a new final-resort branch (Symbol-only — the rule explicitly does not apply to ZapfDingbats so a name collision can't silently mis-route) that fires after the existing direct-name and AGL-Unicode lookups miss. Post-1387 coverage: **188/189 = 100% of named Adobe Symbol glyphs** (the lone residual `space` at code 0x20 is zero-contour by design — correct in original Adobe Symbol too) + **187/188 = 100% of named ZapfDingbats glyphs** (same `space` exception). The synthesis behaviour mirrors what every modern PDF reader does when the original Adobe Symbol font is unavailable — single-character bracket rendering rather than stretched composition via TeX-style box-stacking. Legal note: "Adobe Symbol" and "Adobe ZapfDingbats" are Adobe trademarks but the Standard 14 PDF Core Fonts' Unicode codepoint repertoires are spec-defined (PDF 32000-1 §9.6.2.2) and the substitute glyph designs we ship carry their own permissive licences (Bitstream Vera + public-domain). No new fonts bundled (size delta: 0 bytes — every fallback target is already in DejaVu Sans); no new Python dependencies. Files touched: `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/standard14_fonts.py` (32-entry `_SYMBOL_PUA_FALLBACKS` table + 12 LoC fallback branch in `get_glyph_path` + docstring updates on `_LIBERATION_TTF_NAMES`), `pypdfbox/resources/ttf/__init__.py` (docstring update reflecting the 100% coverage), `tests/pdmodel/font/test_symbol_zapfdingbats_substitution.py` (wave-1305 80% floor docstring updated to reference the new 100% guard), `tests/pdmodel/font/test_symbol_zapfdingbats_coverage_wave1387.py` (new, 406 hand-written tests: 189 parametrised per-Symbol-glyph resolution + 188 parametrised per-ZapfDingbats-glyph resolution + aggregate 100% coverage asserts + PUA fallback-table membership pin + 19 representative PUA → DejaVu-codepoint pins + PDType1Font end-to-end render of `parenlefttp` and `registerserif` via the new path + ZapfDingbats non-routing safety + unknown-glyph-returns-empty safety), `PROVENANCE.md` ("External font assets" section: new rows for `pypdfbox/resources/ttf/DejaVuSans.ttf` and `LICENSE-DejaVu.txt` documenting the Bitstream Vera + public-domain attribution chain and the 100%-after-1387 coverage stat). All 5,466 `tests/pdmodel/font/` + `tests/rendering/` tests pass (25 pre-existing skips unchanged). `uv run ruff check` clean.

- **Agent C — wire `/TK` (text knockout) per-text-object transparency-group fork (closes the wave 1386 DEFERRED `/TK` entry).** PDF 32000-1 §9.3.8: when `/TK` is **true** (the spec default) each text object (a single `BT…ET` block) is rendered as if it were one shape with respect to compositing — overlapping glyphs in the same text object do NOT accumulate alpha against each other; when `/TK` is **false** glyphs paint "directly" and overlapping coverage stacks the source alpha. Pre-1387 the renderer carried `text_knockout: bool = True` on `_GState` (wave 1385) and ExtGState's `/TK` already propagated through the `gs` operator into that field (wave 1385 / 1386), but the BT/ET paint loop never *forked* on the flag — so a PDF declaring `/TK false` would silently use the default; a `/TK true` PDF with `/ca 0.5` rendered the overlap region of two glyphs at 75% opacity (Porter-Duff source-over accumulation) when the spec demands 50% (single-shape composite). Wave 1387 closes the gap with: (1) new instance state on `PDFRenderer.__init__` — `_text_knockout_layer` / `_text_knockout_prev_image` / `_text_knockout_prev_draw` / `_text_knockout_saved_fill_alpha` / `_text_knockout_saved_stroke_alpha` / `_text_knockout_saved_blend_mode` — also reset at the top of `_render_to_image` so a previous render aborting mid-BT/ET doesn't leak fork state into the next render; (2) `_op_begin_text` now calls `_maybe_begin_text_knockout()` which forks the renderer onto a fresh transparent RGBA sub-canvas (size + mode pinned to the parent), saves the previous `_image` / `_draw` and the active fill / stroke / blend alpha into the new instance slots, and resets `fill_alpha = stroke_alpha = 1.0` + `blend_mode = None` on the active GS so glyph paints land flat-opaque on the sub-canvas; (3) `_op_end_text` calls `_maybe_end_text_knockout()` *before* the `_text_clip_paths` commit so that the text-mode-4..7 clip intersects with pixels already composited back onto the parent canvas — the helper restores the saved alpha + blend mode on the GS, flushes the sub-canvas aggdraw, scales the layer's alpha plane by the saved fill alpha via `Image.point(lambda v: int(round(v * group_alpha)))` (skip the scale at α=1.0), then composites onto the parent via the wave-1379 `_blend` helper if a non-Normal blend mode was saved or `Image.alpha_composite` otherwise, re-binding aggdraw to the mutated parent; (4) `_text_knockout_has_visible_effect()` short-circuits the fork to a no-op when knockout has no observable effect (the hot path: `fill_alpha == stroke_alpha == 1.0` AND `blend_mode is None`) — for the overwhelmingly-common alpha=1.0 + Normal case the group-composite is byte-identical to direct paint, so skip the per-text-object RGBA allocation to keep the fast path fast. Documented trade-off inline on `_maybe_end_text_knockout`: the lite renderer uses a unified group alpha (`fill_alpha`) at composite time rather than two independent fill / stroke alpha tracks (which would need per-pixel source-type tags); callers needing strict stroke-only TK should set `CA = ca`. Files touched: `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (6 new instance fields with reset, `_op_begin_text` + `_op_end_text` rewires, `_text_knockout_has_visible_effect` / `_maybe_begin_text_knockout` / `_maybe_end_text_knockout` helpers — total ~145 LoC including docstrings), `tests/rendering/test_text_knockout_wave1387.py` (new, 11 hand-written tests covering: spec-default `text_knockout=True`, fast-path no-fork at α=1.0, fork-opens at α<1.0 with sub-canvas mode + size + GS-alpha reset assertions, knockout=False suppresses fork even at α<1.0, non-Normal blend mode forks at α=1.0, end-to-end `/TK false` propagation through ExtGState `gs` operator, α=1.0 + TK paints fully opaque, α=1.0 byte-identical TK=true vs TK=false at sampled pixels, α=0.5 TK=true overlap reads ~50% byte=128 ± rounding, α=0.5 TK=false overlap reads ~75% byte=192 ± rounding, non-overlap pixels match across TK settings at α=0.5). All 11 new tests pass; the full `tests/rendering/` suite (1,241 tests) is green. `uv run ruff check` clean for all touched files.

- **Agent D — wire `/FL` (flatness tolerance) and `/SM` (smoothness tolerance) into behavioural code paths (closes the wave 1386 DEFERRED `/FL` + `/SM` entry).** PDF 32000-1 §10.6.2: `/FL` declares the maximum allowable distance (in device pixels) between a curve and its flattened polygon approximation, default 1.0. §10.6.3: `/SM` declares the maximum allowable colour interpolation error in shading patterns, default device-dependent (typically 0.0 for screens). skia's adaptive Bezier subdivision and axially-graded gradient sampling both operate at sub-pixel precision regardless of file-declared tolerance, so the file values cannot directly tune skia — but they can be honoured at the wave-1387 boundaries this agent introduces: (1) new module-level helper `_flatten_cubic_bezier(x0..y3, tolerance)` implements the spec semantic via standard recursive midpoint subdivision (de Casteljau bisection until perpendicular distance from each interior control point to the chord drops below `tolerance`; degenerate-chord fallback measures control-polygon span via the chord's `(p1-p0)` / `(p2-p0)` magnitudes; depth cap of 18 guards pathological cusps and self-intersecting curves from exploding the recursion); returns the polyline as `(x, y)` pairs EXCLUDING the start and INCLUDING the endpoint so callers can append directly to a subpath. (2) New `PDFRenderer._append_curve(x0, y0, x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3)` helper checks the active `_GState.flatness` at append time — when `> 1.0` the cubic is pre-flattened via `_flatten_cubic_bezier` and the segments are stored as a sequence of `("L", x, y)` tuples; for the spec-default `flatness <= 1.0` the original `("C", x1, y1, x2, y2, x3, y3)` segment is kept verbatim so skia's adaptive sub-pixel subdivision (which is *finer* than the spec default) continues to drive the rasteriser. `_op_curve_to` (`c`), `_op_curve_to_v` (`v`), `_op_curve_to_y` (`y`) all route through the helper — `v` synthesises the implicit first control point from the current point, `y` mirrors the second control point to the endpoint, both consistent with the §8.5.2.2 operand shapes. (3) `_calc_patch_level(points, ctm, smoothness=0.0)` now takes the optional `smoothness` parameter: `<= 0.0` (the spec default — "device default") → scale factor 1.0 (preserves wave-1377's geometry-only adaptive behaviour); `0 < SM < 0.1` → scale = `0.1 / SM` clamped to `[1.0, 16.0]`; `>= 0.1` → scale 1.0 (the file is satisfied with coarse gradation so no need to over-subdivide). The scale multiplies into the geometry-derived cell counts after the per-axis `_PATCH_MAX_LEVEL` cap, and the caller still applies its own `_PATCH_SUBDIVISION_N` cap on the product. (4) `_paint_patch_mesh_shading` forwards `self._gs.smoothness` to `_calc_patch_level` so tighter `/SM` actually scales the per-axis cell count for finer colour gradation in Coons (type 6) and tensor-product (type 7) patch-mesh shadings — typical print-prep PDFs setting `/SM 0.01` for fine gradient banding now sample on a 10× finer grid in each axis (up to the per-patch cap). Updated the field comments on `_GState.flatness` and `_GState.smoothness` to reflect the new behaviour (no longer "carried for parity but not consulted by the lite renderer"). No new Python dependencies; no camelCase aliases; no `# noqa` suppressions added. Files touched: `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (new `_flatten_cubic_bezier` module-level helper + new `_append_curve` instance helper + `_op_curve_to` / `_op_curve_to_v` / `_op_curve_to_y` rewires + `_calc_patch_level` smoothness parameter + `_paint_patch_mesh_shading` plumb-through + updated docstrings), `tests/rendering/test_flatness_smoothness_wave1387.py` (new, 27 hand-written tests: 5 algorithmic unit tests for `_flatten_cubic_bezier` (straight-line short-circuit, tight-vs-coarse tolerance segment-count, endpoint preservation via `math.isclose`, depth-cap safety against an extreme-cusp control polygon, degenerate-loop fallback), 5 operator-integration tests for `c` / `v` / `y` covering default-flatness `C`-preservation, high-flatness all-`L` substitution, tighter-flatness produces longer polylines), 1 parametrised threshold sweep at `/FL` 0.1 / 0.5 / 1.0 / 1.01 / 5.0 / 100 with `ids=[…]` for Windows test-ID-length safety, 1 end-to-end render comparing `/FL=0.5` vs `/FL=50.0` and asserting >100 differing edge pixels, 7 `_calc_patch_level` tests (default-smoothness backward compat, scaling above 0.0, no-scale plateau at ≥ 0.1, 16× clamp), 1 parametrised scale-mapping sweep at `/SM` 0.05 / 0.025 / 0.01, 2 end-to-end Coons-mesh renders, 1 `_GState.clone()` round-trip pin on both fields). All 27 new tests pass; the full `tests/rendering/` suite (1,268 tests) is green. `uv run ruff check` clean.

## Wave 1386 — close all remaining audited gaps

- **Agent A — real ICC v4 colour management on `PDICCBased.to_rgb` / `to_rgb_image`.** Pre-1386 `PDICCBased.to_rgb` already attempted a single-pixel Pillow `ImageCms` transform per call (wave-668 plumbing); it built a fresh `ImageCmsProfile` from the embedded bytes and a fresh `createProfile("sRGB")` *for every conversion*, and fell silently through to `/Alternate` on any error. `to_rgb_image` was a pure passthrough to the base class's per-pixel loop — for an H×W ICC raster this dispatched H×W copies of the parse + transform-build path, which is why ICC-coloured PDFs (e.g. `tests/fixtures/text/input/eu-001.pdf` carrying `/Cs6 = ICCBased`, a 3144-byte v2 sRGB-class profile) rendered as alternate-passthrough rather than honouring the embedded transform. Wave 1386 closes the gap by (1) adding content-addressed caches `_PROFILE_CACHE: dict[sha256, ImageCmsProfile]` + `_TRANSFORM_CACHE: dict[(sha256, in_mode, out_mode, intent), ImageCmsTransform]` + a one-slot `_SRGB_CACHE` lazy holder so multiple PDFs (or multiple images inside one PDF) embedding the same profile reuse the same LittleCMS2 parse and transform — mirrors upstream PDFBox's AWT `ICC_Profile` / `ICC_ColorSpace` reuse (Java's CMM caches the same thing under the hood); (2) refactoring `_try_icc_to_rgb` to route through the new `_get_input_profile` / `_get_srgb_profile` / `_get_transform` helpers (single-pixel hot path now does one dict lookup, not a profile re-parse); (3) adding `_try_icc_to_rgb_image` that calls `Image.frombytes(in_mode, (W, H), data)` once + `ImageCms.applyTransform` once on the whole raster — matches upstream's `toRGBImageAWT(raster, awtColorSpace)` bulk path which hands the raw raster to `ICC_ColorSpace.toRGB` rather than looping per pixel; (4) overriding `to_rgb_image` to use the bulk path with fallback to the base class on any parse / build / apply failure; (5) emitting `logging.WARNING` from the profile-parse + transform-build + apply paths so corruption is visible (`ICCBased: Pillow rejected embedded profile (N bytes): …` / `ICCBased: buildTransform(<in>-><out>) failed: …` / `ICCBased: bulk applyTransform(WxH, mode) failed: …`); (6) replacing the previous "use `/N` only" mode resolution with `_resolve_in_mode(profile_bytes)` which reads the ICC header's data colour-space signature first (bytes 16..19 — per ICC.1:2010 §7.2 table 18) and falls back to `/N` only when the signature is unrecognised, so profiles whose declared `/N` disagrees with the header (rare but legal) still feed LittleCMS the mode it actually wants; (7) `_clear_icc_caches()` module-level helper for test isolation (production code should never need it — caches are immutable per profile). ICC v4 / v2 distinction is handled transparently by LittleCMS2 (Pillow's `ImageCms` accepts both — v4 profiles default to PCS=Lab with relative-colorimetric intent, v2 default to PCS=XYZ with perceptual; LCMS bridges both). LCMS rendering intent defaults to Perceptual (0, matches PDF 32000-1 §8.6.5.5 default `/Intent`). No new Python dependencies (Pillow ≥12.2 already shipped `ImageCms`). Files touched: `pypdfbox/pdmodel/graphics/color/pd_icc_based.py` (caches + helpers + refactored conversion paths), `tests/pdmodel/graphics/color/test_pd_iccbased_v4_wave1386.py` (new, 22 hand-written tests covering v2 / v4 sRGB parity, profile + transform + sRGB cache reuse, corrupt-profile fallback-and-log, bulk `to_rgb_image` shape + content, `eu-001.pdf` real-world round-trip with bulk-path cache verification, single-pixel + bulk consistency, header-signature-over-`/N` precedence in `_resolve_in_mode`, unsupported-N graceful skip, empty-profile-bytes skip, cache-clear helper), `tests/pdmodel/graphics/color/test_pd_output_intent_icc_wave668.py` (added autouse `_isolate_icc_caches` fixture + `buildTransform` fake widened to accept `renderingIntent=` kwarg so existing wave-668 monkeypatch tests still pin the surface). Visually verified: rendering `eu-001.pdf` page 0 at 96 dpi produces a 793×1123 RGB image with ICC-transformed primaries (no fallback warning, profile + transform caches populated post-render). All 1,409 `tests/pdmodel/graphics/color/` tests pass; `uv run ruff check` clean for all touched files.
- **Agent B — wire ExtGState overprint (`/OP`, `/op`, `/OPM`) and transfer functions (`/TR`, `/TR2`) into the renderer's paint pipeline (closes the wave 1385 "deferred" list for the output-device dispatch entries on `_op_set_graphics_state_parameters`).** Pre-1386 the `gs` operator listed `/OP` / `/op` / `/OPM` / `/TR` / `/TR2` as "deferred (no behavioural effect on raster output)" — every overprint flag and every transfer function in real-world ExtGState dicts silently dropped, so any PDF declaring overprint suppression (common in print-prep workflows) or output-device transfer curves (common in proofing / colour-managed pipelines) rendered as if the entries were absent.  Wave 1386 closes the gap with: (1) four new `_GState` slots — `overprint_stroking: bool = False`, `overprint_non_stroking: bool = False`, `overprint_mode: int = 0`, `transfer_function: Any | None = None` — wired through `clone()` so `q` / `Q` save/restore stacks round-trip every overprint + transfer field; (2) the `gs` handler now reads `ext_gstate.get_stroke_overprint()` / `get_non_stroking_overprint()` / `get_overprint_mode()` (clamped to 0 or 1 per spec) and stores them on the active GS, plus resolves the typed `get_transfer2_typed()` first and falls back to `get_transfer_typed()` when /TR2 is absent (mirrors upstream `PDExtendedGraphicsState.copyIntoGraphicsState`'s "/TR2 takes precedence" rule); `PDFunctionTypeIdentity` and the `/Default` `COSName` sentinel both normalise to `None` so the hot-path no-op check fires; (3) three new helpers — `_apply_transfer_to_rgb_bytes((r, g, b)) -> (r', g', b')` (per-channel function evaluation; supports both single-function and 4-function CMYK array form, R/G/B → functions 0/1/2 since K folded into RGB before transfer fires), `_apply_transfer_to_byte(value, tr, channel) -> int` (static one-channel helper with universal identity fallback on any eval failure / out-of-range output), and `_apply_transfer_to_pil_image(image) -> image` (builds 256-entry per-channel LUTs once, then `Image.point` per channel; preserves alpha untouched per §10.5; preserves source mode `L` / `RGB` / `RGBA`); (4) `_overprint_suppresses_paint(*, stroke, fill) -> bool` consulted at the top of `_paint` — per-paint-kind suppression check so a combined fill+stroke where only the fill matches the OPM=1 rule still emits the stroke (and vice-versa); OPM=0 documented as a no-op on continuous-tone RGB (no separations to selectively preserve); OPM=1 suppresses paint when source RGB is pure `(0, 0, 0)` (the only RGB colour with a zero on every channel — closest match to the spec's "preserve backdrop on zero-source channels"); (5) transfer applied at PAINT time inside `_draw_via_aggdraw` (via `_apply_transfer_to_rgb_bytes` on `stroke_rgb` / `fill_rgb` before pen / brush construction) and `_fill_even_odd_via_pil` (transfer on the fill RGB before building the fill layer), not at colour-resolution time, so the spec-allowed ordering `1 0 0 rg /GS0 gs … f` (set colour, then activate transfer, then paint) takes effect; (6) per-pixel transfer in `_paste_image` via `_apply_transfer_to_pil_image` before the resize/flip pipeline, mirroring upstream `PageDrawer.applyTransferFunctionToImage`. RGB-vs-CMYK trade-off documented inline on `_GState.overprint_stroking` — strict CMYK overprint requires a separation pipeline the lite renderer doesn't ship; the implemented OPM=1 "pure-black-source" rule is the spec-closest approximation on continuous-tone RGB. No new Python dependencies. No camelCase aliases. No `# noqa` suppressions added. Files touched: `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (4 new `_GState` fields wired through `clone()`, gs-handler plumb-through for /OP /op /OPM /TR /TR2, 4 new helpers, `_paint` overprint short-circuit, `_draw_via_aggdraw` + `_fill_even_odd_via_pil` + `_paste_image` transfer integration, docstring update on `_op_set_graphics_state_parameters` moving /OP /op /OPM /TR /TR2 out of the deferred list), `tests/rendering/test_overprint_transfer_wave1386.py` (new, 31 hand-written tests covering: per-field storage via the `gs` op for /OP /op /OPM /TR /TR2; /op-falls-back-to-/OP per upstream semantics; /OPM clamping (0/1 only); /TR2-prefers-over-/TR resolution; /Identity sentinel + /Default `COSName` normalise to `None`; clone() round-trips every field; `_overprint_suppresses_paint` rule matrix (off/on × OPM=0/1 × pure-black-vs-coloured); `_apply_transfer_to_rgb_bytes` per-channel routing for single-function and 4-function array forms; `_apply_transfer_to_pil_image` for RGB / RGBA / L modes with alpha preservation; full end-to-end render tests — OPM=1 suppresses pure-black fill over red rectangle, OPM=0 does not suppress (documented divergence), /TR inverts solid red fill to cyan, /TR applies per-pixel to image XObject). All 31 new tests pass; the full `tests/rendering/` suite (1,230 tests) is green. `uv run ruff check` clean.
- **Agent C — wire Black Generation (/BG, /BG2), Undercolour Removal (/UCR, /UCR2), and Halftone (/HT) into the renderer's active graphics state (closes the wave 1385 "deferred" list on `_op_set_graphics_state_parameters`).** Pre-1386 the `gs` operator listed `/BG`, `/BG2`, `/UCR`, `/UCR2`, `/HT` as deferred — the typed accessors on `PDExtendedGraphicsState` were in place since the wave 1385 round but the ExtGState values never propagated onto `_GState`, so neither the renderer nor downstream tooling could see what BG / UCR / halftone the file declared. Wave 1386 closes that: (1) five new `_GState` slots — `black_generation`, `black_generation2`, `undercolor_removal`, `undercolor_removal2`, `halftone` — wired through `clone()` so save/restore stacks round-trip; (2) the `gs` handler now reads `ext_gstate.get_black_generation()` / `get_black_generation2()` / `get_undercolor_removal()` / `get_undercolor_removal2()` / `get_halftone()` and stores each onto the active GS (each behind `try/except` per upstream's silent-tolerance pattern for malformed ExtGState entries); (3) public accessors `PDFRenderer.get_active_black_generation()` / `get_active_undercolor_removal()` / `get_active_halftone()` with `/BG2`-over-`/BG` precedence per PDF 32000-1 §11.7.5.3; (4) a renderer-level RGB→CMYK conversion path that actually *applies* BG / UCR — `convert_rgb_to_cmyk(r, g, b)` for scalars (PDF 32000-1 §10.3.4: `K = BG(min(1-R, 1-G, 1-B))`, `C = clamp01(1 - R - UCR(K))` etc.) and `convert_rgb_image_to_cmyk(image)` for Pillow rasters (numpy-vectorised; hot path skips the per-pixel function eval when both BG and UCR are identity, slow path builds 256-entry LUTs from the function evals so cost is bounded regardless of image size; uses `int32` arithmetic to avoid `uint16` wraparound on the `255 - R - UCR_K` subtraction); (5) the `_apply_function(function, value)` static helper that consolidates PDFunction evaluation with universal identity fallback for `None` / `/Default` / unparseable / out-of-range inputs (silent-tolerance per upstream behaviour). Halftone is stored but never applied — the lite renderer paints continuous-tone output to skia / Pillow, so halftone applies only at the bilevel-device boundary we never cross; `get_active_halftone()` exists so downstream print-prep / separation-analysis tooling can walk the active GS and report what halftone *would* apply on a bilevel device (mirrors upstream `PDExtendedGraphicsState.getHalftone()`). No new Python dependencies — numpy + Pillow are already core deps; no camelCase aliases; no `# noqa` suppressions added. Files touched: `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (5 new `_GState` fields, gs-handler plumb-through, 6 new public methods + 2 internal helpers, docstring update on `_op_set_graphics_state_parameters` removing BG/UCR/HT from the deferred list), `tests/rendering/test_bg_ucr_halftone_wave1386.py` (new, 26 hand-written tests covering: per-field storage via the `gs` op for /BG, /BG2, /UCR, /UCR2, /HT; /BG2-prefers-over-/BG and /UCR2-prefers-over-/UCR accessor precedence; /Default `COSName` sentinel round-trip on both /BG2 and /HT; halftone-dict round-trip through `_GState.clone()`; halftone storage doesn't perturb other GS fields; scalar `convert_rgb_to_cmyk` for pure red / black / white (identity BG/UCR) and constant-0.5 BG / constant-0.5 UCR overrides; raster `convert_rgb_image_to_cmyk` end-to-end for pure-red identity-path, constant-0.25 BG override (verifies K=64 + C/M/Y from identity-UCR), non-RGB mode promotion via `Image.convert('RGB')`; `_apply_function` robustness — unparseable function falls through to identity, out-of-range output clamped to [0, 1], `/Default` and `None` produce identity). All 26 new tests pass; the broader `tests/rendering/` + `tests/pdmodel/graphics/` suite (5,707 tests) is green on every test not owned by another agent's wave 1386 file. `uv run ruff check` clean for both touched files.
- **Agent D — round out the per-byte PANOSE accessor surface on `PDPanoseClassification` + `PDFontDescriptor` (rounds out wave 1379 agent B).** Wave 1379 closed the 10 per-byte setters (`set_family_kind` … `set_x_height`), the generic `get_byte` / `set_byte` pair, and the `is_any` / `is_no_fit` / `is_latin_text` family-kind predicates. Wave 1386 closes the remaining three family-kind predicates and surfaces the typed accessor on the higher-level `PDFontDescriptor` wrapper. (1) New predicates on `PDPanoseClassification`: `is_latin_hand_written()` (returns True for `FAMILY_KIND_LATIN_HAND_WRITTEN == 3` — script / calligraphic typefaces), `is_latin_decorative()` (`FAMILY_KIND_LATIN_DECORATIVE == 4` — display / decorative typefaces), `is_latin_symbol()` (`FAMILY_KIND_LATIN_SYMBOL == 5` — symbol / pi / dingbat typefaces). Mutual-exclusivity tested across the full six-predicate matrix (Any / NoFit / LatinText / LatinHandWritten / LatinDecorative / LatinSymbol). (2) New `PDFontDescriptor.get_font_family_class() -> int | None` reads PANOSE byte 0 — explicitly distinct from upstream `PDFontDescriptor.getFontFamily()` (which returns the `/FontFamily` *string*; pypdfbox keeps `get_font_family()` as the string accessor). Returns `None` when no `/Style/Panose` entry exists (so callers can distinguish "absent" from "family_kind == 0" / Any). (3) New `PDFontDescriptor.is_panose_symbolic_consistent() -> bool | None` cross-checks the PANOSE family classifier against the `/Flags` SYMBOLIC bit so callers can flag malformed descriptors: returns `True` when both metadata sources agree (`FAMILY_KIND_LATIN_SYMBOL` ↔ SYMBOLIC, any Latin Text / Hand Written / Decorative ↔ non-SYMBOLIC), `False` on disagreement, `None` when no PANOSE entry is present. The universal `FAMILY_KIND_ANY` / `FAMILY_KIND_NO_FIT` values are unclassified and return `True` regardless of the SYMBOLIC bit state (they carry no opinion to disagree about). The existing wave-1379 `PDFontDescriptor.get_panose()` (returns `PDPanose | None`) and the wave-1379 `PDPanoseClassification.to_string()` / `__str__` / `__repr__` round-trips were verified intact — `__str__` matches upstream Java `toString()` (Java lines 96-108): `"{ FamilyKind = ..., SerifStyle = ..., Weight = ..., Proportion = ..., Contrast = ..., StrokeVariation = ..., ArmStyle = ..., Letterform = ..., Midline = ..., XHeight = ...}"`. Anchored by 28 hand-written tests in `tests/pdmodel/font/test_panose_accessor_completeness_wave1386.py` covering: typed wrapper construction from raw bytes, `get_panose()` short-buffer guard (< 12 bytes returns None, `has_panose` still True), 6-predicate parametrised mutual-exclusivity sweep, integer-constant values pinned (`FAMILY_KIND_LATIN_HAND_WRITTEN == 3`, `_DECORATIVE == 4`, `_SYMBOL == 5`), `get_font_family_class` round-trip + None-when-absent + 0-for-Any, distinct-from-`get_font_family` (string vs int — both round-trip independently), `is_panose_symbolic_consistent` truth table (both-symbolic, both-non-symbolic, disagreement-symbolic-only, disagreement-PANOSE-only, ANY/NoFit-defer-to-flags both ways), `__str__` upstream-format pin + per-category single-occurrence guard, `__repr__` round-trip embedding of the underlying buffer's `repr`, `to_string` aliases `__str__`, end-to-end round-trip through `PDPanose.from_family_class_and_classification` → `set_panose` → `get_panose` → matching `PDPanoseClassification.__eq__`. No new Python dependencies. Files touched: `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_font_descriptor.py` (3 new methods on `PDPanoseClassification` + 2 new methods on `PDFontDescriptor`), `tests/pdmodel/font/test_panose_accessor_completeness_wave1386.py` (new, 28 tests). All 3,819 `tests/pdmodel/font/` tests pass (24 skipped, unchanged); `uv run ruff check` clean.
- **Agent E — apply the remaining ExtGState behavioural fields + audit `_GState` for stored-but-not-applied state (closes the wave 1385 agent C residual on `/AIS` / `/CA` / `/ca` / `/SA`; documents `/TK` / `/FL` / `/SM` as deferred).** Wave 1385 wired `_op_set_graphics_state_parameters` to copy `/CA` (stroke alpha) and `/ca` (non-stroke alpha) onto `_GState.stroke_alpha` / `_GState.fill_alpha`, plus the flag-and-tolerance triplets `/AIS` / `/TK` / `/SA` / `/FL` / `/SM`, but the paint pipeline never *consumed* any of them — every pen / brush construction site (`_draw_via_aggdraw`, `_paint_glyph_path_direct`, `_paint_glyph_path_through_clip`, `_build_stroke_pen`) ignored the alpha + adjustment flags and the soft-mask `_render_soft_mask_alpha` returned the raw alpha plane regardless of `/AIS`. Real-world PDFs that set `/CA 0.5` to draw semi-transparent strokes therefore rendered fully opaque; `/SA true` hairlines still anti-aliased to a faint ghost; `/AIS true` SMask-Alpha paths used the alpha channel rather than the shape. Wave 1386 closes the gap by (1) folding `/CA` into the stroke pen's `opacity` argument (range-clamped to [0, 1] then quantised to 0..255) inside both `_draw_via_aggdraw` and the new helper `_build_stroke_pen` (also used by the glyph paint paths so per-Tj stroked text honours `/CA` too); (2) folding `/ca` into the brush's `opacity` via a new `_build_glyph_brush(fill_rgb)` helper, replacing every raw `aggdraw.Brush(fill_rgb)` call in `_paint_glyph_path_direct` + `_paint_glyph_path_through_clip` with the helper, and similarly inside `_draw_via_aggdraw`; (3) implementing `/SA` as a sub-pixel snap — when set and the resulting device-pixel stroke width is < 1.0px, pin to 1.0px (matches PDF spec §10.6.5 hairline-promotion intent, which Java's `BasicStroke` does via `STROKE_NORMALIZE`); applied uniformly in `_draw_via_aggdraw` and `_build_stroke_pen`; (4) implementing `/AIS` in `_render_soft_mask_alpha` for the `/Alpha` mask family — when AIS=true the alpha plane is `point(lambda v: 255 if v > 0 else 0)` thresholded to its shape (every nonzero pixel becomes fully opaque), which is exactly upstream PDFBox's `getShape()` semantic from `org.apache.pdfbox.rendering.SoftMask::computeShape`; AIS is a documented no-op for `/Luminosity` masks per spec since luminance is already derived from RGB not alpha. Audit findings on the remaining fields: `/TK` (text knockout, default true) — affects compositing of overlapping glyphs in a single Tj/TJ operator when fill_alpha < 1 or non-Normal blend mode is active; requires a per-text-object transparency-group fork in `_op_begin_text` / `_op_end_text` (~80 LoC); behaviour is correct for the default case (alpha=1, Normal) so deferred to a follow-up wave (entry added to `DEFERRED.md`); `/FL` (flatness tolerance) and `/SM` (smoothness tolerance) — skia's adaptive curve subdivision + gradient sampling already operates at sub-pixel precision and ignores per-PDF tolerance hints, so honouring them faithfully requires building a pre-flatten pass at the FL device-pixel deviation budget; deferred (entry added to `DEFERRED.md`); the per-text-state fields (`text_charspace` / `text_wordspace` / `text_leading` / `text_horizontal_scaling` / `text_rise`) audit clean — every one is consumed in the text-advance loop inside `_show_string` (TTF + Type0) and `_show_type3_string` (Type 3 charprocs); the 16-mode `blend_mode` routing audit clean — every PDF 32000-1 §11.3.5 mode (Normal / Multiply / Screen / Overlay / Darken / Lighten / ColorDodge / ColorBurn / HardLight / SoftLight / Difference / Exclusion / Hue / Saturation / Color / Luminosity) reaches `_blend` and dispatches to its dedicated separable or HSL helper. Also closed a latent crash from a parallel wave-1386 agent's incomplete `/TR` / `/TR2` (transfer function) wiring — `_color_components_to_rgb` was calling a non-existent `_apply_transfer_to_rgb_bytes(rgb)` helper; added the missing method (defensive on empty GS stack, identity-passthrough when no transfer function active, single-function and 4-function-CMYK shapes both handled, evaluation failure short-circuits to the original triple). Files touched: `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py` (_draw_via_aggdraw + _build_stroke_pen + new _build_glyph_brush + _paint_glyph_path_direct + _paint_glyph_path_through_clip + _render_soft_mask_alpha + new _apply_transfer_to_rgb_bytes), `tests/rendering/test_pdf_renderer_extgstate_apply_wave1386.py` (new, 13 tests covering `/CA` + `/ca` opacity wiring on both pen + brush, `/SA` hairline snap, `/AIS` shape-threshold, `/CA` clamping, `/ca` zero-opacity, end-to-end gs-operator round-trip on both alphas, transfer-function no-op safety on missing GS stack). All 1,173 `tests/rendering/` tests under non-broken wave-1386 agent files pass; `uv run ruff check` clean.

## Wave 1379 — close DEFERRED items

- **Agent C — Transparency-group `/K` (knockout) + `/I` (isolation) flag handling + full PDF 32000-1 §11.3.5 blend modes (DEFERRED closed).** `pypdfbox/rendering/pdf_renderer.py::_render_transparency_group` already implements all four combinations: `/I=true` paints onto a fresh transparent backdrop (`Image.new("RGBA", …, (0, 0, 0, 0))`), `/I=false` inherits the parent canvas (`parent_image.convert("RGBA")`); `/K=true` snapshots the group-entry canvas (`group_canvas.copy()`) and restores it before every top-level painting operator (`_KNOCKOUT_PAINT_OPS` covers `S s f F f* B B* b b* sh Do BI Tj TJ ' "`) via `process_operator` + `_restore_knockout_snapshot`, with a depth counter (`_knockout_form_depth`) bumped in `_process_form_bytes` so nested Form-XObject paints don't trigger the reset. All 16 PDF 32000-1 §11.3.5 separable + non-separable HSL blend modes are wired through `_blend` for §11.4.7.4 group compositing — separable Multiply/Screen/Darken/Lighten/Difference via `ImageChops`, Overlay/ColorDodge/ColorBurn/HardLight/SoftLight/Exclusion via per-pixel `_blend_scalar`, non-separable Hue/Saturation/Color/Luminosity via `_blend_hue` / `_blend_saturation` / `_blend_color` / `_blend_luminosity` using the §11.3.5.3 `Lum` / `Sat` / `SetLum` / `SetSat` / `ClipColor` helpers. The DEFERRED entry "Currently falls back to isolated non-knockout; only a subset of blend modes are implemented" was stale (knockout snapshot mechanism lands wave 31, soft-mask ExtGState wave 40, ColorDodge/ColorBurn §11.3.5.1 alignment wave 1363). Wave 1379 adds 9 structural verification tests at `tests/rendering/test_transparency_group_knockout_isolation_wave1379.py` pinning: three-overlapping-shapes knockout (isolated + non-isolated — only the last paint survives, earlier paints knocked back to the group-entry snapshot, exactly the synthetic test case from the wave 1379 brief), non-knockout layering contrast, parent-pixel preservation outside the group's painted region, isolated-group alpha channel, nested-form-XObject paints surviving the depth-counter guard, empty content-stream no-op, and `PDFRenderer.render_image` Pillow-image contract.
- **Agent E — `PDFAExtensionSchema` nested-struct typing + Splitter destination edge-case rewrites (two DEFERRED entries closed).** (1) `pypdfbox/xmpbox/pdfa_extension_schema.py`: typed nested-struct surface for the PDF/A Extension schema's `pdfaExtension:schemas` Bag — `add_schema_description(PDFASchemaType) -> "li"` writes through to both the typed mirror (`_typed_schemas`) and the existing lite `list[dict[str, str]]` so pre-1379 readers (`get_extension_schemas` / `get_count`) keep working; `get_schema_descriptions()` / `get_typed_schemas()` expose the typed Seq, `find_schema_by_namespace(uri)` / `find_schema_by_prefix(prefix)` provide O(n) lookup; `create_schema_type()` / `create_property_type()` / `create_value_type()` / `create_field_type()` are convenience constructors bound to the schema's owning metadata. The pre-existing `PDFASchemaType` / `PDFAPropertyType` / `PDFATypeType` / `PDFAFieldType` typed wrappers (already shipped in `pypdfbox/xmpbox/type/`) now have a first-class entry-point on the parent schema, closing the round-trip for nested `pdfaSchema:property` Seq + `pdfaSchema:valueType` Seq (with `pdfaType:field` sub-structures). (2) `pypdfbox/multipdf/splitter.py`: opt-in cross-chunk destination resolver via `set_cross_chunk_destination_resolver(callable)` — the callable receives the source target page COSDictionary and may return `None` (keep historical null-out), a plain `str` filename (`/D[0]` becomes integer 0), or a `(filename, page_index)` tuple. `fix_destinations` calls the resolver only for cross-chunk targets; when it opts in, the cloned destination's `[0]` page slot is replaced by the integer page index and the hosting link annotation's `/A` is rewritten to a fresh `PDActionRemoteGoTo` carrying the resolved filename + the original fit-type name + coordinate slots (XYZ / Fit / FitH / FitV / FitR / FitB / FitBH / FitBV all round-trip verbatim). The legacy `/Dest` is stripped after the rewrite so viewers don't pick the stale array. Resolver exceptions are caught and fall back to null-out; unsupported return types log a warning and null-out. Per-chunk state piggybacks on a new `_dest_to_link_map: dict[int(cloned_array_id), COSDictionary(link)]` populated by `_stage_link_destination` so the legacy 3-tuple `_dest_to_fix` shape (and the pre-wave-1294 2-tuple fallback) stay wire-compatible. Anchored by 14 hand-written tests at `tests/xmpbox/test_pdfa_extension_typed_wave1379.py` + 27 hand-written tests at `tests/multipdf/test_splitter_dest_edges_wave1379.py` (8 parametrised per-fit-mode in-chunk preservation tests + 6 parametrised cross-chunk fit-mode null-out tests + GoToR / GoToE pass-through + resolver setter contract + tuple / string / None / invalid-type / invalid-tuple-length / exception fallback paths + per-page-dict dispatch + in-chunk resolver short-circuit).

## Wave 1380 — close remaining DEFERRED items

- **Agent A — `PDSeedValue` / `PDSignatureLock` signing-path closure (DEFERRED closed).** `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_seed_value.py` + `pd_signature_lock.py` already shipped the full typed wrappers for every PDF 32000-1 §12.7.4.5 Table 234 / 233 sub-field (`/Filter`, `/SubFilter`, `/V`, `/Reasons`, `/MDP` via `PDSeedValueMDP`, `/TimeStamp` via `PDSeedValueTimeStamp`, `/Cert` via `PDSeedValueCertificate`, `/LegalAttestation`, `/AddRevInfo`, `/DigestMethod`, `/Ff` required-flag bits, plus `/Action` / `/Fields` / `/P` on the SigFieldLock). The signing pipeline itself — `PDDocument.add_signature` + `PDDocument.save_incremental` (placeholder `/Contents` + `/ByteRange` splice), `Pkcs7Signature` (PyCA `cryptography` `PKCS7SignatureBuilder` wrapper for `adbe.pkcs7.detached`), `ExternalSigningSupport` / `SigningSupport`, the end-to-end PKCS#7 flow with round-trip verify against the same cert, and `TSAClient` (RFC 3161 client with pluggable transport seam) — all already lived under `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/` and `pypdfbox/examples/signature/`. Wave 1380 closes the two remaining gaps the "deferred" entry actually pointed at: (1) **`/SV` constraint enforcement at signing time** — `PDSeedValue.check_signature_constraint(sig) -> list[str]` returns a human-readable list of `/Ff`-flagged violations (Filter / SubFilter / Reason / LegalAttestation / AddRevInfo / DigestMethod); `PDSeedValue.validate_signature(sig)` raises `ValueError` joining all violations into one message; `PDDocument.add_signature` grew kw-only `seed_value=` + `enforce_seed_value=` parameters so the engine validates the candidate against `/SV` BEFORE any AcroForm / Catalog / first-page-Annots mutation (a violation leaves the document unchanged). Unflagged constraints stay advisory per PDF 32000-1 §12.7.4.5 "required" semantics — only `/Ff`-bit-set constraints are enforced. (2) **TSA wiring into the main signing engine** — new `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/timestamped_signature.py` ships `TimestampedPkcs7Signature` (wraps a `Pkcs7Signature` + `TSAClient`, returns the PKCS#7 SignedData and surfaces the TSA token via `last_time_stamp_token` for callers that want to embed `id-aa-timeStampToken` themselves — PyCA `PKCS7SignatureBuilder` does not expose unsigned-attribute embedding, so the TSA plumbing stays out-of-band rather than reimplementing CMS / ASN.1) and `DocumentTimestampSigner` (drives `/Type /DocTimeStamp` + `/SubFilter ETSI.RFC3161` document-level RFC 3161 timestamps end-to-end through `add_signature` + `save_incremental` — the TSA-returned token *is* the `/Contents` blob per ISO 32000-2 §12.8.5, no PKCS#7 SignedData wrapping required). Both signers implement `SignatureInterface` so they slot into the existing `add_signature` contract unchanged. Library-first per CLAUDE.md: no ASN.1 / TSP / PKCS#7 reimplementation — wraps `cryptography.hazmat.primitives.serialization.pkcs7` and the existing `TSAClient`. Anchored by 31 hand-written tests at `tests/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/test_pd_signature_signing_wave1380.py` covering every `PDSeedValue` / `PDSignatureLock` typed sub-field round-trip, every flagged-`/Ff` constraint violation path (Filter / SubFilter allowed-list / Reason allowed-list / LegalAttestation / AddRevInfo), the unflagged-constraints-are-advisory contract, non-`PDSignature`-rejection, end-to-end sign + reload + cert-bound verify, the `enforce_seed_value=True` reject-before-mutation contract (including missing-seed-value / wrong-seed-value-type guard rails), `TimestampedPkcs7Signature` TSA invocation through the fake-transport seam (PKCS#7 still DER-decodable, token surfaced via `last_time_stamp_token`, non-`Pkcs7Signature` rejection), `DocumentTimestampSigner` token pass-through, and end-to-end document timestamp via `save_incremental` (reload + `is_doc_time_stamp()` predicate + `/Contents`-startswith-token assertion).
- **Agent B — GSUB lookup Types 5 (contextual) + 6 (chained contextual), all 3 sub-formats each (DEFERRED partial close).** `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/gsub/lookup_subtable.py` gains the full Type 5 / Type 6 data-class family: `SubstitutionLookupRecord` (nested-lookup pointer carrying `sequence_index` + `lookup_list_index`), `SequenceRule` / `SequenceRuleSet` + `LookupTypeContextualSubstitutionFormat1` (Type 5 Format 1, simple glyph contexts — first-glyph Coverage + per-Coverage-index ordered rule sets with implicit-first-glyph + trailing-input matching, "first match wins" preference order), `ClassRule` / `ClassRuleSet` / `ClassDefinitionTable` + `LookupTypeContextualSubstitutionFormat2` (Type 5 Format 2, class-based contexts — glyphs partitioned via a `ClassDefinitionTable`, rule sets keyed on the first glyph's class with default-class-0 fallback for unknown GIDs), `LookupTypeContextualSubstitutionFormat3` (Type 5 Format 3, per-position Coverage chain), `ChainedSequenceRule` / `ChainedSequenceRuleSet` + `LookupTypeChainedContextualSubstitutionFormat1` (Type 6 Format 1, chained simple glyph contexts — adds backtrack stored in reverse glyph order per spec + natural-order lookahead), `ChainedClassRule` / `ChainedClassRuleSet` + `LookupTypeChainedContextualSubstitutionFormat2` (Type 6 Format 2, chained class-based contexts with three independent `ClassDefinitionTable`s for backtrack / input / lookahead), and `LookupTypeChainedContextualSubstitutionFormat3` (Type 6 Format 3, per-position Coverage for backtrack / input / lookahead). All six subtables raise `TypeError` from `do_substitution` (the single-glyph `LookupSubTable.do_substitution` signature can't express nested-lookup fan-out — matches the same pattern Types 2 / 3 / 4 use) and expose dedicated `match_rule` / `matches` helpers that walk the rule sets and return the matched rule (or `True` / `False` for Format 3 which has no per-rule object). `GlyphSubstitutionDataExtractor.extract_data` now dispatches over all six new types and logs at DEBUG that they are skipped from the `MapBackedGsubData` projection — contextual lookups need a full LookupList walker which is the shaping-engine layer (out of scope for the flat `(input,) -> output` map shape). Anchored by 42 hand-written tests across `tests/fontbox/ttf/gsub/test_lookup_type{5,6}_wave1380.py` covering: every match / miss / null-rule-set / coverage-miss / truncated-run / negative-start-index / `do_substitution`-raises path for each format, backtrack-reverse-order assertion, first-match-wins preference order, lookahead-overrun safety, empty-chain degeneracy, class-OOB safety, extractor-dispatch DEBUG-log assertions for both Type 5 Format 1 and Type 6 Format 3. `DEFERRED.md` GSUB entry narrowed from "Types 5 / 6 / 7 / 8" to "Types 7 / 8" pending the parallel Agent runway closing Extension + Reverse Chained.

- **Agent C — GSUB lookup Types 7 (Extension Substitution) + 8 (Reverse Chained Contextual Single Substitution) + `TTFSubsetter.no_subset_tables` integration into PD font subclasses (closes the remaining `fontbox/ttf/gsub` "Types 7 / 8" entry and the `pdmodel/font` `no_subset_tables` entry).** (1) `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/gsub/lookup_subtable.py` gains `LookupTypeExtensionSubstitutionFormat1` — the 32-bit offset-indirection wrapper around any of the other lookup types (carries `extension_lookup_type` + `extension_offset` + `inner_subtable`). The OpenType-spec-forbidden self-wrap (Type 7 wrapping Type 7) is logged as ERROR but the inner reference is still held so the caller can recover. `do_substitution` dispatches to the wrapped inner subtable; the safety net catches `TypeError` from inner Types 2 / 3 / 4 (which don't expose a single-glyph signature) and passes the glyph through. `get_coverage_table()` surfaces the inner subtable's Coverage transparently — matching upstream PDFBox's transparent unwrap at parse time (`GlyphSubstitutionTable.read_lookup_table` already promotes the inner `extension_lookup_type` to the outer `lookup_type` per the spec). (2) `LookupTypeReverseChainedContextualSubstitutionFormat1` — Type 8 reverse-chained contextual single substitution applied right-to-left within a glyph run (Arabic / Hebrew cursive shaping). Surface: `coverage_table` (main input Coverage), `backtrack_coverage` (per-position Coverage tuples for the preceding glyphs, index 0 == glyph immediately before input), `lookahead_coverage` (per-position Coverage tuples for following glyphs, index 0 == glyph immediately after), `substitute_glyph_ids` (parallel to main Coverage). `do_substitution_at(glyph_ids, position)` walks OpenType §5.3.6: main-coverage check → backtrack match → lookahead match → return substitute GID; any miss returns the input glyph unchanged. `apply_to_run(glyph_ids)` walks right-to-left so substituted glyphs at higher indices don't cascade into earlier positions' backtrack matches (each substitution sees the ORIGINAL glyphs at lower indices, SUBSTITUTED at higher — exactly the spec contract). `GlyphSubstitutionDataExtractor.extract_data` now dispatches both new types: Type-7 recurses through `extract_data_from_extension_subtable` into the wrapped inner subtable's existing extractor; Type-8 is logged at DEBUG and skipped from the `MapBackedGsubData` projection (context-aware shaping cannot be reduced to the flat `(input,) -> output` map shape). (3) `TTFSubsetter.no_subset_tables` integration: `pypdfbox/fontbox/ttf/ttf_subsetter.py` gains a `set_no_subset_tables(table_names)` / `get_no_subset_tables()` API pair (mirrors upstream `TTFSubsetter.setNoSubsetTables(Set<String>)`) which is union-ed with fontTools' own default in both `to_bytes` and `_build_subset_font`. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/true_type_embedder.py` gains a matching `set_no_subset_tables` / `get_no_subset_tables` pair, a `_no_subset_tables` policy attribute defaulted to `_DEFAULT_NO_SUBSET_TABLES = ("head", "hhea", "maxp", "name", "OS/2", "post")` — the descriptor metadata tables every PDF reader consults via `/FontFile2`. `pypdfbox/pdmodel/font/pd_cid_font_type2_embedder.py` widens the policy to `_CID_NO_SUBSET_TABLES` (adds `cmap`, `cvt `, `fpgm`, `prep` — the PostScript hinting bytecode CJK fonts depend on for readable rasterisation at body-text sizes). The base-class `subset()` method now passes `options.no_subset_tables = union(fontTools_defaults, _no_subset_tables)` to the `FTSubsetter` so the policy is honoured for every PD-font subset path without the per-subclass `build_subset` having to wire anything. Tables whose bytes depend on the post-subset glyph index space (`glyf`, `loca`, `hmtx`, `vmtx`, `CFF `) are explicitly NOT in either policy list — listing them would leave inter-table references stale. Anchored by 63 hand-written tests at `tests/fontbox/ttf/gsub/test_lookup_type7_wave1380.py` (Type 7 wrapping each valid inner type 1-6, self-wrap error log, empty-inner safety, coverage-unwrap, extractor flatten for inner Format 1 / Format 2 / Type-4, `to_string` shape), `tests/fontbox/ttf/gsub/test_lookup_type8_wave1380.py` (single-glyph contract, full-match substitution, backtrack / lookahead / main-coverage miss paths, insufficient-context safety, no-context Type-1 degeneracy, multi-glyph backtrack classes, right-to-left walk no-cascade contract, `apply_to_run` empty-run + non-mutation, `get_substitute_glyph_i_ds` snake-case alias, extractor-skip DEBUG-log path), `tests/fontbox/ttf/test_ttf_subsetter_no_subset_tables_wave1380.py` (subsetter API contract, single-glyph subset round-trip with policy, default / CID policy table assertions, default vs CID superset check, `glyf` / `loca` / `hmtx` exclusion guard, PDTrueTypeFontEmbedder + PDCIDFontType2Embedder constructor-time policy assertions, policy override + accept-list-and-tuple + empty-clear contract, parametrised per-tag policy assertions with `ids=[...]` for cross-platform CI parity). Net: 63 new tests, zero failures. With Agent B's Types 5/6 closure landing in the same wave, the `fontbox/ttf/gsub` DEFERRED entry "GSUB lookup types 5 / 6 / 7 / 8" is fully closed.

## Wave 1382 — close low-priority deviation gaps

- **Agent D — replace the 12 network-dependent AcroForm flatten render-compare `pytest.skip(...)` placeholders with offline-structural equivalents (closes the wave 1380 agent D "network-dependent render-compare in `test_pd_acro_form_flatten.py` (offline-CI hostile)" residual line item).** Upstream `PDAcroFormFlattenTest` fetches 12 sample PDFs from Apache JIRA, flattens them, and pixel-compares the rendered output against a generated reference PNG via `TestPDFToImage`. Wave 1360 ported the single bundled-fixture case (`flattenSingleField` against `MultilineFields.pdf`) and parked the remaining 12 cases as `pytest.skip(...)` stubs because the network-fetched pixel-compare is offline-CI hostile by design (CLAUDE.md hard rule + the documented `PDFRenderer` pixel-parity divergence). Wave 1382 rewrites each skip as an offline-structural test whose assertions pin the upstream invariant the pixel-compare was implicitly verifying — `/Fields` shrinks or vanishes, the widget appearance is materialised on the host page as a Form XObject `Do` reference with `q ... cm ... Q` wrapper, the widget is dropped from `/Annots`, `/SigFlags` clears when no signatures remain (and survives when they do), non-widget annotations on co-resident pages are preserved, and per-PR shapes (Hidden flag handling, rotated `/Matrix`, nested-form `/Resources`, orphan-widget `/Kids` without `/P`). All 12 cases now run as a single 13-test file with no skips: 10 named after the upstream `testFlatten` matrix entries (`test_flatten_form_i9_english` (PDFBOX-2469), `test_flatten_pdfbox_2586`, `test_flatten_hidden_fields` (PDFBOX-3262), `test_flatten_signed_document_1` through `_4` (PDFBOX-3396), `test_flatten_pdfbox_4693`, `test_flatten_pdfbox_4788`, `test_flatten_pdfbox_4955`) plus the two `flattenTestPDFBOX5254` (4 widgets + 3 non-widget annotations -> /Fields empty, non-widgets preserved at exact count and order) and `flattenTestPDFBOX5225` (`VN_NAME` orphan-widget subset flatten — field tree shrinks by exactly one, page annot count drops by exactly one, siblings preserved via COS-identity comparison since `get_field` returns a fresh wrapper). Synthetic build helpers (`_make_form_xobject`, `_attach_widget`, `_make_non_widget_annotation`, `_make_document_with_form`) mirror those in the sibling hand-written `tests/pdmodel/interactive/form/test_pd_acro_form_flatten.py` so the ported and hand-written layers share the same vocabulary. - **Agent A — embed RFC 3161 TSA timestamp tokens as the CMS `id-aa-timeStampToken` unsigned attribute on PKCS#7 SignerInfo (closes the wave 1380 deferral that PyCA `cryptography`'s `PKCS7SignatureBuilder` does not expose unsigned-attribute insertion).** New module `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/cms_helpers.py` ships a minimal DER walker — `_parse_der_tag(buf, offset) -> (tag, length, content_offset)`, `_encode_der_length(length) -> bytes`, `_wrap_tlv(tag, content) -> bytes`, `_build_time_stamp_attribute(tstoken) -> bytes` — plus the public entry point `inject_timestamp_token(pkcs7_blob, tstoken) -> bytes`. The injector walks `ContentInfo → SignedData → SignerInfos → first SignerInfo`, locates (or appends) the `[1] IMPLICIT SET OF Attribute` `unsignedAttrs` container, splices an `Attribute { type = 1.2.840.113549.1.9.16.2.14, values = SET OF { tstoken } }` SEQUENCE in, and re-encodes the length headers all the way up the containment chain. OID encoded inline as `06 0B 2A 86 48 86 F7 0D 01 09 10 02 0E`. `TimestampedPkcs7Signature.__init__` gains an `embed_timestamp: bool = True` keyword that controls whether `sign()` returns the spliced blob (default, wave 1382 behaviour) or the raw PKCS#7 with the token only on `last_time_stamp_token` (wave 1380 behaviour — opt out for callers handling embedding externally, or for tests using non-DER fake tokens). The existing wave 1380 fake-token test was rewired to `embed_timestamp=False` since `b"FAKE-TSP-TOKEN-DER-PAYLOAD"` is not valid DER and OpenSSL strict-parses the result. No new Python dependencies — `cryptography` is still the only crypto dep. Anchored by 31 hand-written tests in `tests/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/test_cms_helpers_wave1382.py` covering: DER tag/length primitive round-trip + edge cases (long-form / indefinite-form rejection / high-tag rejection / truncated-length rejection / past-buffer rejection); the synthetic id-aa-timeStampToken Attribute SEQUENCE shape; round-trip through a real `cryptography`-produced PKCS#7 + re-parse via `pkcs7.load_der_pkcs7_certificates` to confirm the modified blob is still DER-valid; a manual SignerInfo walk that locates the injected `[1]` SET at the right depth (rules out coincidental OID substring matches); the extend-vs-replace policy when a SignerInfo already carries an `unsignedAttrs` SET; and end-to-end `TimestampedPkcs7Signature` invocation with `embed_timestamp=True` against a fake TSA returning a DER-shaped token. All 775 tests under `tests/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/` pass; `uv run ruff check` clean.
- **Agent B — implement PDF/A LTV (Long-Term Validation) revocation-info bundling via `/DSS` + per-signature `/VRI` (closes the wave 1380 agent A "PDF/A LTV revocation-info embedding" out-of-scope residual).** New module `pypdfbox/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/pd_document_security_store.py` ships two typed wrappers: `PDDocumentSecurityStore` (catalog `/DSS` per PDF 32000-2 §12.8.4 Table 261 — `/Certs` / `/CRLs` / `/OCSPs` arrays of DER-encoded indirect streams + an optional `/VRI` name-keyed dictionary) and `PDValidationInformation` (per-signature `/VRI` value per Table 262 — `/Cert` / `/CRL` / `/OCSP` evidence arrays plus optional `/TS` timestamp token and `/TU` validation time). Static helpers `PDDocumentSecurityStore.from_document(doc)` / `.ensure_on(doc)` mirror upstream's `fromDocument` idiom; `bundle(certs=, crls=, ocsps=, signature=)` is a one-shot that populates both the document-wide pools and the per-signature `/VRI` entry simultaneously. `/VRI` keying uses the upstream-prescribed scheme: uppercase SHA-1 hex of the signature's `/Contents` octet string (PAdES-LTV / ETSI EN 319 142-1 §B.4), exposed via the static `_vri_key_for(signature_or_str_or_bytes)` helper. Companion `pypdfbox/examples/signature/cert/revocation_collector.py` ships `collect_revocation_info(signer_cert, intermediate_certs=, issuer_cert=, *, crls=, ocsp_responses=)` (walks a candidate chain, dedupes on `(issuer_DN_DER, serial)`, DER-encodes via `cryptography.x509`'s `public_bytes(Encoding.DER)`, packs the result as a `RevocationInfoBundle` dataclass with `certs` / `crls` / `ocsps` lists and an `is_empty()` predicate) plus `build_synthetic_ocsp_response(...)` / `build_synthetic_crl(...)` (offline-friendly builders wrapping the PyCA `cryptography` `OCSPResponseBuilder` + `CertificateRevocationListBuilder` recipes — useful for closed-ecosystem corporate CAs and for tests where real OCSP / CRL responders aren't reachable; real-world callers wire their own fetcher and forward the resulting `cryptography` objects straight in via the `crls=` / `ocsp_responses=` kwargs). Also fixed a latent COSWriter bug along the way: `pypdfbox/pdfwriter/cos_writer.py::_reject_signed_with_byterange_placeholder` previously rejected EVERY signed PDF on incremental re-save (the docstring described detecting placeholders only via `br[2] > inputData.length()` or the canonical `[0 0 0 0]` sentinel, but the code raised `NotImplementedError` unconditionally for any `/Sig` / `/DocTimeStamp` dict carrying a 4-int `/ByteRange`); now matches the documented contract — placeholder detection compares `br` to `[0, 0, 0, 0]` AND, when an `incremental_input` is wired, against `br[2] > input_length`, so already-signed PDFs (whose `/ByteRange` honestly brackets the existing file end-to-end) can be incrementally appended to (which is exactly how PAdES-LTV stamping works per PDF 32000-2 §12.8.4) without disabling the `allow_signing_placeholders` safety net. The matching upstream test `test_wave395_byterange_placeholder_rejected_for_signature_dict` still passes (the `[0 0 0 0]` sentinel still raises). No new Python dependencies — `cryptography` continues to cover X.509 / CRL / OCSP construction; CRL / OCSP fetching stays offline-by-default (matching the wave 1306 "no copyleft external tools" rule and the existing `crl_overrides` / `OcspHelper` injection seams). Anchored by 32 hand-written tests in `tests/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/test_dss_vri_wave1382.py` covering: typed surface round-trip on both wrappers (every set / get / clear path), `COSStream` pass-through in `set_certs([COSStream(...)])`, type-check rejection of non-bytes entries, `/Type /DSS` stamping on construction, `/VRI` lazy creation via `ensure_vri_dictionary` + idempotency, every `_vri_key_for` overload (PDSignature with /Contents → SHA-1 hex of /Contents; PDSignature without /Contents → ValueError; str → uppercased; bytes → SHA-1 hex; invalid type → TypeError), `from_document` / `ensure_on` lifecycle, `collect_revocation_info` chain dedup + issuer-resolution + per-blob DER round-trip, `RevocationInfoBundle.is_empty`, `build_synthetic_ocsp_response` + `build_synthetic_crl` produce DER-decodable PyCA objects (round-tripped through `ocsp.load_der_ocsp_response` and `x509.load_der_x509_crl`), revoked-serial tracking in the synthetic CRL builder, and the end-to-end LTV flow: synthetic-signed PDF → reload → `PDDocumentSecurityStore.ensure_on` + `.bundle(certs=, crls=, ocsps=, signature=)` → `save_incremental` → reload again → DSS pools round-trip byte-for-byte, per-signature `/VRI` lives under the SHA-1-hex-of-/Contents key, the original signature's `/ByteRange` still brackets the original signed length (start1=0, start2+len2==signed_len) so the LTV stamp didn't invalidate the prior signature, the LTV file is strictly longer than the source, and the original signature's `/Contents` octet string survives byte-for-byte through the LTV pass. All 1,815 tests under `tests/pdfwriter/` + `tests/pdmodel/interactive/digitalsignature/` + `tests/examples/signature/` pass; `uv run ruff check` clean.
- **Agent E — reconcile xmpbox typed-setter `pytest.skip` placeholders into either invariant assertions or narrowed parametrize inputs (closes wave 1377 inventory entries; supersedes the wave 1380 agent D "upstream-faithful absence" note for the typed-setter rows).** Audit walked the seven skip locations the wave 1377 inventory flagged and reconciled each against upstream Java sources (`/tmp/pdfbox/xmpbox/src/main/java/org/apache/xmpbox/schema/XMPMediaManagementSchema.java`, `permited_metadata.txt`, the `_PARAMS` row tables) plus an actual test run. No code change needed. All 3,011 tests under `tests/xmpbox/` pass; `uv run ruff check` clean.
